Guo Takes Martyrs' Remains Back to Beijing 58

Japanese Consul in Jinan Also Sends Telegram Back to Country Reporting

Jinan Correspondence: As of this (27th) morning, the remains of the May 3rd martyrs in the back garden of the former Foreign Affairs Office have been completely unearthed and are all packed in a large jar. The May 3rd Martyrs Commemoration Committee originally had a temporary plan to temporarily place the remains in the old Foreign Affairs Office. Guo Jingluan, however, gave up her family and career and has been working for several years to achieve this little success. She is not very satisfied with a hasty temporary placement. At 9 a.m. this morning, she personally visited Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, and told him of her intentions, stating that she would take them back to Nanjing and ask important figures from the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to read them and determine a proper aftermath. In the future, when the Martyrs' Tomb is completed here, they can still be transported back for formal burial to comfort the loyal souls. She believes that no matter whether there are remains of Martyr Cai among them, she greatly admires the loyal remains of those who sacrificed for the country. She feels uneasy unless she carries them with her before they are formally buried. Han expressed his approval of this. Guo then hurried back to the old Foreign Affairs Office, took two photos of the remains, and included all the workers who participated in the excavation, the guards, and visitors as a memorial. After the photography was completed, the remains were packed in a leather bag and taken to the car. The remains of all the martyrs who died at the time are completely contained in this one package. According to Ms. Guo, Martyr Cai has a son named Haizhu, who is nine years old, and a daughter named Lili, who is eight years old. Both are studying at Qixiu Primary School in Shanghai.

The sixth meeting of the May 3rd Martyrs Commemoration Committee was held yesterday (26th) at 5 p.m. at the Jiaoji Hotel. The attendees were Zhang Honglie, Lu Tingzhuan, Wen Chenglie, Xing Jiantian, Guo Jingluan, and those attending in an observational role were Zhang Zhenfu. The meeting was chaired by Zhang Honglie and resolved: (1) The martyrs' ashes will be packed in a magnetic jar and temporarily buried. (2) Engineers will be sent to inspect the location of the construction of the Martyrs' Tomb. The location will be designed by Director Zhang. (3) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs will be informed of the excavation situation. After the burnt remains of the May 3rd martyrs were found, the Japanese here were extremely alarmed. The Japanese Consul in Jinan, Nishida, has sent a detailed telegram to the Japanese government reporting everything. (27th)

Disaster Situation is Serious in Various Counties of Southern Shanxi 59

Victims Go Out to Find Food

Garrison Troops Transport Grain to Save Themselves

Shang Zhen Is Planning Relief

Taiyuan Correspondence: In the various counties of southern Shanxi, disasters of soldiers, bandits, and drought have occurred one after another. The residents are exhausted, and nine out of ten houses are empty. Bandits are unable to supply military needs, and even the people's food will be cut off. Therefore, the disaster victims, unable to maintain their livelihoods, have joined together in groups to go to other provinces to find food. Grain prices in various places have soared, changing several times a day. Those without money are sitting and waiting to die, and even those with money have no way to buy it. Song Zheyuan, therefore, seeing that food is lacking in the garrison areas of each army and that the supply of military rations is particularly difficult, fearing that once it is cut off, accidents will occur, sent personnel to Tianjin to purchase 10,000 bags of flour and to Xinyang to purchase 18,000 bags of wheat. He has now requested the Deputy Ministry to order the Railway Bureau to prepare cars to transport them to the area for relief. According to Song's plan, he intends to continue this method. On the one hand, it can maintain military food, and on the other hand, it can reduce and stabilize grain prices. The various members of the Provincial Government, seeing that the situation in southern Shanxi is becoming more and more serious, held a conversation meeting with representatives in the Provincial Government a few days ago to exchange relief opinions. Regarding the issue of military pay, it has been decided that on the one hand, the Provincial Government will be urged to handle the grain and fodder loan to repay the arrears, and on the other hand, counties without garrisons will continue to assist counties with garrisons to temporarily maintain the current situation. Although the principle has been approved, the specific methods are difficult to determine. The voices of opposition to the grain and fodder loan from the various counties in northern Shanxi have recently intensified, and whether this move can be accomplished is a question. It is also a question as to where the funds for the counties without garrisons to assist the counties with garrisons will come from and how they will be repaid. Provincial Chairman Shang Zhen has returned from Beiping yesterday and immediately stated that he will find ways to provide relief for this major problem in southern Shanxi and is scheduled to convene representatives today and tomorrow to negotiate definite measures. (22nd)

The Construction of the Hei-Sui Railway in Heilongjiang Province is Imminent 60

Funding Determined to be 30 Million Yuan

Vast Coalfields Discovered in Daqingshan

Harbin Dispatch: The section of railway from Suihua to Heligang in eastern Heilongjiang Province is a planned extension of the Hu-Hai Railway. It passes through the four counties of Tieli, Qingcheng, Tangyuan, and Mulan, with a total length of 789 kilometers. Except for the mountainous terrain between Qingcheng and Tangyuan, which makes construction more difficult, the rest is all plains, making track laying and foundation building extremely easy. The engineering survey was conducted last winter by a survey team organized by the Hu-Hai Railway, with two surveys conducted before and after, and the route was changed twice. The plan has now been finalized. The Heilongjiang Provincial Government plans to use 30 million yuan for the construction of the railway, including all bridge and culvert construction costs along the route. The cost of purchasing vehicles, etc., is not included in this amount. However, the source of the funds, whether through attracting commercial investment, local fundraising, or allocation from the provincial treasury, has not yet been determined. Given the current financial situation of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, it is practically impossible to raise such a large sum. According to the proposal of Gao Yunkun, the general manager of the Hu-Hai Railway, half of the funds would be allocated by the Hu-Hai Railway, and the other half would be raised locally by the four counties of Mulan and Tangyuan that the route passes through. There will be no separate engineering bureau established; the Hu-Hai Railway will be responsible for the construction. The Hegang Coal Mining Company has been operating prosperously in recent years, but the coal produced must rely on waterways for transportation. In winter, due to the freezing of the waterways, it must be transported by large vehicles, which greatly affects sales. Therefore, there is talk of automatically raising some funds to assist the Hu-Hai Railway in quickly building this line. The Heilongjiang Provincial Department of Construction will hold a meeting on this matter at the end of this month to determine the source of the funds, and then construction will begin immediately. It is expected that the track can be laid by early spring next year, and at the latest by the end of 1933 (the 22nd year), the railway can be opened to traffic. After this road is completed, it will not only provide convenience for the people and businesses in the eastern wilderness of Heilongjiang Province and promote local benefits, but it will also greatly facilitate transportation for the counties of Huachuan and Yilan on the south bank of the river.

The Northeast Daqingshan in Hailun County, eastern Heilongjiang, covers an area of 35 square miles and has a huge coalfield. The Heilongjiang Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines sent the technical expert Han Shutang to investigate the area a month ago. Han used new drilling methods and spent a month. He has now passed through Harbin and returned to the province.

It is said that a total of six drills have been completed, and it is expected that more than ten drills will be needed for success. Based on the six drills, nineteen layers have been discovered. The coal quality appears to be tertiary lignite, similar to the famous Muling coal in the Northeast in terms of oil content and heating power. The coal area produces 170,000 tons of coal per year, which can supply mining for at least 70 years. The current exploration team has already built wooden houses in the mountains to continue the exploration work. However, after mining begins in the future, transportation will be inconvenient, and it will be extremely difficult to transport the coal out. The area is more than eighty miles away from the Hailun Station of the Hu-Hai Railway. Even if a branch line is built, it can only reach the foot of the mountain. The coalfield is in the mountains, so how to transport the coal to the foot of the mountain is also a problem. The Heilongjiang Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines has decided to recruit commercial investment after the exploration results are obtained to establish the Daqingshan Coal Mining Co., Ltd., a joint public-private venture, to carry out mining. (23rd)

Tragedy Occurs in Harbin 61

The Murderer is the Cousin of the Eastern Railway Director Fan Qiguang

Unable to Force a Prostitute to Elop, He Lured Her to a Hotel and Murdered Her

Harbin Dispatch: A shocking murder case occurred here the day before yesterday (the 20th). The murderer is a young man of about twenty years old, and the victim is a prostitute. After the crime, the murderer fled, but left behind photos and other items. The Chinese and Japanese military and police agencies have been searching with these photos, and it is expected that the case will be solved soon. The details of this matter are roughly as follows:

The Murderer is an Eastern Railway Employee: The murderer's name is Fan Xusui, courtesy name Jinqing, from Changzhou, Jiangsu Province. He is 26 years old and currently works as a clerk in the Transportation Department of the Eastern Railway. He is the cousin of the former Eastern Railway Director Fan Qiguang. He graduated from Harbin Institute of Technology. He is tall and handsome, but has a perverse personality. None of his colleagues are close to him. Two years ago, he met the young prostitute Wang Xuehua in the Huifang Shuangfu troupe in Daowai. Wang is 17 years old and from Jiangdu, Jiangsu Province. She lives with her mother, Wang Fengshi, and her younger brother, A San. After Fan met her, they became very close. Most of his salary was spent on her. As of last winter, in addition to what had already been paid, he owed more than 600 yuan in prostitution debts. Xuehua's mother demanded payment from Fan several times, but he never paid. Because of this, Xuehua gradually became distant towards Fan. Last December, Xuehua became pregnant and the fetus was shocked. Fan admitted that it was related to him and sent Xuehua to the Shou Shan Hospital for an abortion. All expenses were supposed to be borne by Fan, but he disappeared afterwards. The hospital refused to release Xuehua, and her mother had to raise money to bring her back. While she was in the hospital, Fan went every night, and always argued with Xuehua. Sometimes he even slapped Xuehua's cheeks. Xuehua endured it with tears because she could not resist. Because of this, the fetus was agitated and eventually miscarried.

Xuehua Breaks Her Promise: Initially, Wang Xuehua, as a prostitute, had told Fan that she was willing to follow him for life. Fan thought it was real. However, when Wang Fengshi demanded payment of the prostitution debts, Xuehua's attitude towards Fan gradually became bleak. Fan realized that she was not sincere, but he continued to perfunctorily appease her, hoping that Xuehua would be moved. Therefore, every time he received his salary, he still went to Xuehua's boudoir, bought her clothes, and often took Xuehua to amusement parks. He took photos with Xuehua, with inscriptions such as "A wife for a wanderer, a pair of pitiful bugs." However, Xuehua's mind was focused only on money, and she continued to feign compliance, not making a hasty break. The day before the Dragon Boat Festival in the lunar calendar, Fan went to the Shuangfu troupe. Wang Fengshi used the festival as an excuse to ask for the debts again. Fan replied that he would pay them off in a day or two. On that day, he paid 30 yuan as a festival bonus, and agreed with Xuehua to go to Sun Island together on the Dragon Boat Festival for a full day of entertainment.

The Course of the Murder: At 8 p.m. on the 20th, Fan went to Xuehua's house, claiming that he had bought clothes for Xuehua and invited her to go out together. Wang Fengshi wanted to go with them,

but was rejected by Fan. They arrived at the Yamato Hotel, owned by the Japanese Terada Junzo, on Shitoudao Street. Fan led Xuehua into room number 1 on the third floor. Then they went out together for dinner. They returned to the hotel at about 10 p.m., obtained the key from the maid, and boiled a kettle of water. Then they entered the room, turned off the lights, and locked the door. At this time, Fan began to discuss eloping with Xuehua. Xuehua refused, and they began to quarrel, the sound reaching outside the door and being heard by the maid. She knocked on the door and asked what was happening. Fan replied that nothing was wrong. At 10:30 p.m., Fan, seeing that Xuehua still refused to elope, became murderous. He took out a dagger from his side and threatened Xuehua. Xuehua tried to scream, but Fan threw her to the ground, straddled her body, and used one hand to strangle her throat, while the other hand vigorously wielded the dagger, stabbing Xuehua's throat, chest, and other parts. Xuehua tried to block with her hands, and her fingers were also injured. Fan stabbed her twenty-three times. Finally, Xuehua screamed tragically and died. At that time, the maid outside heard something strange in the room and peeked from the side of the stairs. By then, Fan had finished his act. He took off his white silk gown, which was stained with blood, left it in the corner of the room, and hurriedly left the room in short clothes without even wearing a hat. He also did not take away the paper box containing his clothes. After Fan left, the maid pushed open the door and entered, and saw Xuehua lying barefoot on the ground, covered in blood and dead. She immediately reported it to the hotel owner, who relayed it to the Japanese consulate police. The Japanese police chief Ogawa then arrived at the scene with many officers and confirmed that Xuehua had died from stab wounds. They then notified the Second Special Police Department, which immediately invited the Special Court to the scene for inspection that night.

The Wounds are Too Horrific to Bear: The Special Court Prosecutor Chuan Ronglin, accompanied by inspectors, came to inspect the body. The wounds of the deceased were as follows: (1) A stab wound three-tenths of an inch wide and five-tenths of an inch deep below the left eyebrow; (2) A two-inch-wide oblique stab wound through the upper right throat; (3) A one-and-two-tenths-of-an-inch wide and two-tenths-of-an-inch deep wound on the upper right chest; there were eleven such wounds; (4) A three-tenths-of-an-inch wide cut wound on the right thumb; (5) Three cut wounds on the upper side of the right arm; (6) A one-inch-wide cut wound on the back of the right hand; (7) A one-inch-long oblique cut wound on the inner side of the left first finger, reaching the bone; (8) A five-tenths-of-an-inch-long cut wound on the inner side of the left second finger, reaching the bone; (9) A one-inch-long and one-inch-deep stab wound on the back of the head on the left side. There were a total of twenty-three wounds and twenty-nine injuries. Xuehua lay face up on the ground, her eyes bulging out, her face covered in blood. The short shirt and pants she was wearing were stained with blood. The tragic scene made onlookers shudder. Among the items left behind by the murderer Fan Xusui was a paper suitcase containing ten Harbin dollars, a diary, a towel, a wooden comb, two porcelain bowls, a bottle of tooth powder, a box of soap, a mirror, eleven portraits, a pair of western pants, a pair of leather shoes, a felt hat, and a blood-stained long gown. Xuehua was wearing a long cheongsam made of blue Indian silk. According to the hotel owner Terauchi, Fan had rented a room in the hotel three times before, and each time he was accompanied by a woman, but each time it was a different woman. He came to book the room on the afternoon of the day of the incident, and deposited a paper suitcase, saying that he would take his family to see a play, and it was late at night and they could not return home, so they borrowed the room for one night. The police station has now moved the body of the deceased Wang Xuehua to the morgue of the municipal hospital. On the 21st, Xuehua's mother, Wang Fengshi, was summoned to inquire about Fan's and Wang's relationship. On the other hand, Fan's photo was distributed to various checkpoints to assist in the arrest. The Japanese police station is also working hard to arrest him because the incident occurred in a Japanese hotel. It is rumored that Fan is hiding in the port area because he has no money. The police station has already set up a plan to investigate. (22nd)

Anqing Airplane Crashes on the Yangtze River in Shashi 62

Damage to the Plane's Parts and Fuselage

Passenger Wang Keming Also Injured

Shashi Dispatch: On June 25th, the China National Aviation Corporation's Anqing airplane, flying from Shanghai to Yichang, had already flown to the skies above Shashi at 4:35 p.m. It was about to turn and descend above Erlangmen, preparing to land on the water and stop. However, the river's current was rapid and the south wind was strong. As the plane approached the water surface, it suddenly overturned. With a loud crash, the plane touched the water and fell into the river, floating downstream for about ten miles. The aircraft after its crash in the Shashi river.

It was rescued by an oil tanker and the customs vessel before being pulled ashore. The plane's parts and fuselage were damaged. Fortunately, both pilots, one Chinese and one American, were unharmed. There was only one passenger, named Wang Keming, who is the manager of the Mingcheng Company in Yichang. He was traveling from Hankou to Yichang. He suffered an external injury to his forehead, and his front teeth were broken. After being carried out of the cabin, he was given first aid and sent to the hospital for treatment. It is said that his life is not in danger. As for the cause of the plane crash, it needs to be investigated and studied before a report can be made. (26th)

Preparations for the Reorganization of the Hankou Municipal Government 63

Hubei Provincial Government Assigns Officials to Draft New Organizational Law

Hankou Dispatch: Regarding the reorganization of the Hankou Municipal Government, the Central Government has previously decided to change it to a municipality under the jurisdiction of the Provincial Government. The Hubei Provincial Government will organize the Municipal Government itself, and the Provincial Government will handle the abolition and retention of various bureaus and offices in accordance with laws and regulations and in consideration of the circumstances. After receiving the order, the Provincial Government submitted it for discussion at the fifth meeting on the 25th and determined three principles: (1) The various bureaus under the Municipal Government, in addition to being merged into the Provincial Government and various departments according to their nature, all other affairs will be handled by departments. (2) Due to the Provincial Treasury's financial difficulties, the expenditure scope of the Municipal Government's funds is stipulated to be between 3,000 yuan and 5,000 yuan. (3) Commissioner Chen Guangzu, Commissioner Wu Guozhen, and Secretary Chuan Xiangrong were designated to be responsible for drafting the organizational outline and budget, and submitting it to the next committee meeting for review and implementation. The reorganization will be implemented no later than July 1st. The position of mayor was originally intended to be filled by Chen Guangzu, but Chen repeatedly stated that he would not take the position. It is rumored that He Baohua will be appointed instead. The specific person will be decided within a day or two. The Hankou Municipal Government was originally directly under the Executive Yuan, with a secretariat, public security, social affairs, public works, education, and finance bureaus, and a health management office. This reorganization aims to simplify the structure. It is rumored that only one secretary and two section chiefs will be set up. The secretariat will be completely abolished. The Public Security Bureau will be directly under the Provincial Government. The social affairs aspects of the Social Affairs Bureau will be merged into the Construction Department, the Finance Bureau into the Finance Department, and the Education Bureau into the Education Department. The Public Works Bureau will be changed to an Engineering Office, and the Health Management Office will remain as is. Wu Guobing is most likely to be the director of the Engineering Office, and Wang Guanhai will remain as the director of the Health Office. Other staff members will be decided by the mayor. (June 26th)

Hankou Garrison Executes Red Bandits by Firing Squad 64

Hankou Dispatch: The Wuhan General Headquarters executed five Red bandits by firing squad on the 25th: Liu Junlong, Wei Rongqing, Liu Fanglin, Pan Jiayu, and Zhan Guangqi. All were sentenced to death in accordance with the Emergency Criminal Law for Endangering the Republic of China and the Provisional Regulations for Punishing Bandits. The charges are recorded as follows: (1) According to the report submitted by Chen Cheng, commander of the 14th Division of the Army, the Red bandits Liu Junlong, Wei Rongqing, and Liu Fanglin, who had infiltrated the army to agitate officers and soldiers, were clearly identified after investigation by the military court. Liu Junlong, also known as Liu Lisan, had a history of misconduct, initially serving as the social liaison for the bandit Xu Chunpu, and later using the power of He Long's bandit army to fine Yue Shang Heng Qilong. He had now infiltrated the 79th Regiment of the 14th Division as a soldier, hoping to agitate officers and soldiers and lead them to join the bandits with their weapons. Wei Rongqing was introduced by Liu and served as a second-class soldier, secretly serving as Liu's secretary and responsible for secret communications. Liu Fanglin had worked under He's bandit army at the lower levels. After joining the army, he was incited by Liu Junlong and served as a liaison officer. This time, he attempted to agitate Zhang Lianfu but was captured. They should all be sentenced to death to serve as a warning. (2) According to the report submitted by the Hankou Public Security Bureau, the Red bandit Pan Jiayu was apprehended. The military court found that the bandit had joined the Communist Party and served as a guerrilla captain. He and Ruan Hanqing and Zhu Tuozi went to Zeng Xianxun's house and demanded a ransom. When they failed to obtain the money, they shot and killed Zeng's grandfather. The plaintiff, Zeng Xianxun, also testified that the facts were consistent. This was a heinous crime and should be sentenced to death as a warning. (3) According to the Hankou Public Security Bureau, the bandit Zhan Guangqi, also known as Zhan Yuwen, from Echeng County, was apprehended and sent for investigation. The military court investigated and requested the Hubei Provincial Government to verify the facts. Subsequently, the Provincial Government and the Echeng County Government's Security Group reported that Zhan Yuwen had colluded with the bandit Wang Shiyu in April of last year to seize weapons from the group several times, killing many civilians. They had also obtained an arrest warrant. It was requested that he be executed quickly to satisfy the people. The defendant was interrogated and confessed without a word. Given his heinous crimes, he should be sentenced to death as a warning. (June 25th)

Resolutions of the Film Review Committee of the Ministry of Interior and Ministry of Education 65

Since the establishment of the Film Review Committee jointly formed by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, the work has been very intense. At the seventh regular meeting of the committee on the 24th of this month, it was further resolved that when applying to the committee for film review, in addition to submitting the required documents (one application form, four copies of the synopsis, and three copies of the cast list) in accordance with the committee's Film Application Review Guidelines, the script of the film should also be submitted (if it is a foreign film, a Chinese translation should be attached). Furthermore, newsreels should also submit a synopsis (if it is a foreign film, a Chinese translation should be attached). It is reported that this resolution has been sent to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to be forwarded to the film companies in the city for compliance.

Regulations on Labor Conscription for River Dredging in 25 Counties in Northern Jiangsu Province 66

The regulations on labor conscription for river dredging in 25 counties in the four prefectures of Huaiyang and Xuhai in northern Jiangsu Province have been approved by the Provincial Government. They are recorded as follows: (Article 1) The Jiangsu Provincial Government is following the Prime Minister's legacy of mandatory labor and has specifically established the Regulations on Labor Conscription for River Dredging. (Article 2) These regulations apply to the dredging of silted rivers within the 25 counties of the four prefectures of Huaiyang and Xuhai in northern Jiangsu Province. (Article 3) Residents of counties, cities, townships, villages, and towns through which rivers pass and who benefit from river dredging have an obligation to participate in the dredging. (Article 4) The implementation of labor conscription shall be organized by a River Dredging Committee composed of the county magistrate, the director of the Construction Bureau, and impartial local gentry in each county, in accordance with the engineering plan and labor conscription rules set by the Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau and under the direction of the Director of the Construction Department. (Article 5) The expenses for labor conscription and river dredging shall be paid from the five-tenths of a water conservancy mu tax collected throughout Jiangsu Province. However, before this mu tax is collected, it will be temporarily advanced from the transport mu tax collected in northern Jiangsu, limited to 100,000 yuan. (Article 6) Subsidies for labor conscription and river dredging in each county shall be determined by the Water Conservancy Bureau at a rate of 10 to 30 yuan per hundred li and submitted to the Construction Department for approval and disbursement. (Article 7) Personnel involved in labor conscription and river dredging may be rewarded or punished by the Provincial Government upon the recommendation of the Construction Department after evaluation by the Water Conservancy Bureau based on their performance. The details will be determined separately. (Article 8) The methods for labor conscription, such as allocating labor per mu or using the industry-food tenant system, will be determined separately. (Article 9) Residents within the labor conscription area who have already been conscripted for road construction this year may apply to the Water Conservancy Bureau to be exempted from river dredging. (Article 10) After the promulgation of these regulations, those who obstruct labor conscription or refuse to comply during implementation may be held liable in accordance with the law. (Article 11) These regulations shall be implemented after being approved and promulgated by the Provincial Government Committee.

Wuhu Express News 67

The Wuhu rice market is related to the commercial and financial affairs of the entire province. After the abolition of Likin, downstream traffic was unimpeded, and many rice merchants directly connected with Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The Wuhu rice market has become virtually stagnant. Recently, purchases by merchants from Hubei in the upper reaches have begun to show some activity. Unexpectedly, the rice industry association today is because of the Grain Transportation Industry Association (i.e., the Guangdong and Chaozhou merchants) has unreasonably added a one-cent remittance fee. The rice industry association requested a reduction or exemption, resulting in a general strike by the transportation industry. Industry representatives Wu Wentang and Jin Shihong, in addition to submitting a petition to the County Chamber of Commerce requesting the cessation of the levy and ordering the association to withdraw from the illegally withheld rapeseed donations from the abolished Anhui and Jiangsu bureaus and abolish all kinds of evils that hinder the rice market, also went to the county government and other agencies to petition for fairness and sanctions.

Business News: A large group of bandits has recently been discovered in Huoqiu County, western Anhui. A telegram has been sent to the Provincial Government requesting the dispatch of troops to block and suppress them as soon as possible to avoid a major disaster.

The local bar association held its regular general meeting today. The meeting discussed the alleged bribery of lawyers She Hongxi and Li Weixin in handling cases, as well as rumors of fraud by judges. As a result of the discussion, it was determined that lawyers She and Li had violated the association's charter, and it was decided to expel them from the association. As for the bribery allegations, they will be filed with the relevant authorities. Chief Prosecutor Deng Zhaoluan attended and spoke, considering it an unfortunate event for the legal community and promising to provide support for a thorough investigation.

Last night at 7:30, Wuhu experienced a heavy thunderstorm, torrential rain, and a hurricane for three hours. Electric lights and telephones were damaged. A house collapsed in Beimen, killing the wife and son of Dr. Wang Jiyan, a total of three people. Wang and another son were seriously injured. Many other houses collapsed in various places, injuring more than twenty people. The godown of the HSBC rice factory collapsed completely, resulting in huge losses. (26th)

Business News: Regarding the issue of Anhui rice exports, the Ministry of Finance recently announced that it would jointly establish an inspection agency with the Anhui Provincial Government. In addition to registration, an inspection fee of six jiao per shi will be levied on exported rice, regardless of whether it is transported by steamship or sailboat. This is currently being discussed. Anhui people believe that this measure will hinder the rice market, and if it becomes a reality, they will swear to fight for it.

The local tax authorities recently received a telegram from Wuyuan reporting that Taibai Town in the county was suddenly attacked and captured by bandits from Jiangxi on the 26th. The entire town suffered heavy losses. The tobacco and alcohol tax bureau was looted, and all employees fled.

Page 10

The Wuhu Guangdong-Chaozhou Tobacco, Ningbo Rice, and Grain Transportation Industry Association has a dispute with the Rice Industry Association over the one-cent remittance fee for rapeseed. Since yesterday, a strike has been implemented. The Public Security Bureau, the County Government, and the County Chamber of Commerce believe that the rice market is extremely important to commerce, people's livelihood, and public order. Therefore, a special emergency meeting was convened at the County Chamber of Commerce at 2 p.m. today. Representatives from both the transportation industry and the rice industry attended. After a long discussion, no resolution could be reached. Finally, it was decided to organize a mediation committee, with Lin Aichen, Zhang Shuqing, and four others representing the transportation industry; Wu Wentang, Jin Shihong, and four others representing the rice industry; and Gu Houfu, Tao Yutang, and four others representing the Chamber of Commerce serving as mediation committee members. The mediation must be completed within three days. The rice market is still at a standstill today.

Regarding the Anhui business tax, the business community in Wuhu has been strongly advocating for it to be levied from July 1st and for the County Chamber of Commerce to notify all associations. The Provincial Finance Department believes that this matter is related to the uniformity of business tax collection throughout the province. Today, it telegraphed the Chamber of Commerce disapproving of this and urging the payment of past taxes. The Chamber of Commerce has scheduled a meeting to discuss this matter in the coming days. (27th)

Local Dispatches 68

Songjiang

Command Headquarters Intercepts Mutinying Soldiers: Recently, soldiers of the Tenth Company, Fourth Battalion, Seventh Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Force staged a mutiny in Xincang Town, Pinghu County, Zhejiang Province. Commander Cao, stationed in Songjiang, immediately dispatched troops to pursue and suppress them, while secretly sending intelligence agents to various ports to track down the mutinying soldiers and prevent them from fleeing. Yesterday, according to intelligence officer Ma Anfu of the Command Headquarters, two suspicious passengers were intercepted on the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer at Zhangyan and brought to the Songjiang headquarters for interrogation. One, Zhang Shiyong from Ningbo, confessed to being a soldier of the said company. He said that as a result of the looting, each person only received five yuan, and the firearms had been discarded in the paddy fields. The other, Fang Fengtian from Jiangxi, confessed the same as Zhang Shiyong. After hearing their confessions, Commander Cao ordered them to be detained and sent to Zhejiang for investigation and handling.

Election of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the County Chamber of Commerce: Yesterday (the 26th), the County Chamber of Commerce held an election for executive and supervisory committee members. The results of the open ballot were announced at 8:00 PM. The elected executive and supervisory committee members are recorded below: (Executive Committee) Cai Zhongyu, Yang Zhimin, Yang Yunshan, Zhang Shengshan, Wu Shengyong, Xie Liangda, Shen Sinan, Zhang Qingquan, Ding Zhouzhi, Wang Xianglin, Zhang Jiliang, Zhang Hanshi, Zhu Yian, Wu Zhengping, Zhang Mengxing (15 people in total). (Supervisory Committee) Zhou Zhuoting, Chen Wenxiong, Hong Songqiao, Xu Yajie, Zhang Fujun, Shi Zhirui, Huang Songxian (8 people in total).

Kidnapper Mao Jinsheng Transferred to Court: Xu Pucheng, the first district chief of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Force, believing that the 20th of this month was the date of the Dragon Boat Festival, and fearing that gatherings of villagers might cause trouble, ordered secret agents to conduct strict investigations. They discovered Mao Jinsheng, a suspicious person, and brought him to the headquarters for interrogation. He confessed that he was from Nantang Township, Nanhui County, and had previously worked under Zhang Yaosheng. In December of last year, he, along with others, using box cannons, kidnapped Sun Xiangyun's wife, Sun Xu, and her younger sister, Sun Amei, in Banqiao Township, Songjiang. He also confessed to having used the ransom money. The district headquarters has already escorted him to the county government for transfer to the county court for investigation and handling according to the law.

Wuxi

Shitangwan Merchant Group Cracks Trafficking Case: Yesterday, the 34th detachment of the Shitangwan Merchant Group in the 16th district (Wan'an City) received a tip-off that Chen Er's house in the Longtan Head shacks in that area was harboring three girls of unknown origin. Upon receiving the report, the group immediately dispatched several members to investigate. Indeed, they found three girls. They immediately took them back to the team for questioning. One, Zhang Jindi, 14 years old, is from Pingkou Donggang, the daughter of Zhang Kezi. Another, Xu Yindi, 10 years old, is the daughter of Xu Xiaolong. The third, Liu Jinfeng, 15 years old, is the daughter of Liu Jizheng and is already engaged as a child bride to Zhou Axing, a resident of Qianzhou Town. According to Chen Er's confession, the three girls were passing through the area at noon on the 25th.

They got lost and wanted to stay overnight, so he took them in. Because the case was strange, the group sent them all to the 15th Public Security Sub-bureau. After preliminary interrogation by Sub-bureau Chief Bao, he ordered the police officers to notify the girls' families to come to the bureau to identify them. Meanwhile, the trafficker Chen Er was sent to the main bureau for investigation and handling.

Robbers Commit Robbery and Shoot the Victim: Shan Peiguan, a villager in Shanjia Tang, about two li east of Zhangjing Bridge in the 7th district (Huai'an City), was over 50 years old. His deceased wife, Yao, had no children, so he adopted A'da (over 30 years old) as his son. A'da married Zhu and had two daughters. Recently, A'da had collected over 300 yuan in membership fees, which was coveted by robbers. On the night of the 27th, around 10:00 PM, the Shan family, both men and women, were enjoying the cool air on the threshing ground because of the hot weather. Suddenly, seven or eight robbers appeared, each armed with a pistol, wearing short clothes, and speaking in a strong northern accent. A'da, seeing the situation, immediately fled. The robbers fired at A'da, fortunately missing him. A'da then hid in a wheat stack, escaping harm. After the robbers entered the house, they saw Shan Peiguan in the kitchen and immediately fired three shots at him. Peiguan was struck by three bullets in the chest and fell beside the water tank, dying instantly. Seeing that their purpose had been achieved, the robbers ransacked the house, and after about an hour, they took the membership money and left to the north. Afterwards, A'da and his wife saw that the robbers were gone and were about to enter the house to check the losses when they saw his father, Peiguan, dead in a pool of blood beside the water tank. They called out to him, but there was no response, and they couldn't help but embrace the body and wail loudly. It was rumored that the robbers who committed this robbery looked like Red Bandits, and fearing they would return for revenge, A'da didn't want to report to the county. At 3:00 PM, he prepared a coffin and buried his father's body. Also, in Buyang Shang, 2nd district (Jingyun City), there is a Chun Shen Jun Grand King Temple, which was built by villager Wan Shengguan, who has a wife and son and lives a poor life. On the night of the previous day, around 11:00 PM, more than ten robbers came with torches and weapons, broke down the door, and dragged Wan from the bed, ordering him not to make a sound. They forced him to reveal the location of the money. Wan replied that he had no money. The robbers then tied him up with ropes and ransacked the chests at will. As a result, they stole ten yuan in cash, two blankets, two sheets, and over twenty pieces of men's and women's clothing. After getting the loot, the robbers left with a whoop.

Economic Pressure Leads to Suicide Attempt, Not Fatal: Jin Taigou, a resident of Qianzhou Town in the 15th district (Qingcheng City), is about 30 years old and has no fixed property. He originally relied on gambling for a living, but now gambling is strictly prohibited everywhere, so he has no income. He and his wife spend their days in sorrow, like oxen facing each other and weeping. The other day, Jin suddenly had thoughts of despair and secretly took a large dose of arsenic, closing his eyes and waiting for death. Later, his wife found out and sent him to the city by boat yesterday to seek treatment at Pu Ren Hospital. His life is not in danger.

The court has investigated and interrogated them several times. It is now heard that the verdict in this case was announced yesterday. Sixty-Year-Old Man Dies Pulling Rickshaw: Yesterday at 9:00 AM, rickshaw puller He Jushu was making a living by pulling a rickshaw. An official from Zhenjiang Customs hired his rickshaw. Because the office hour was approaching, the official couldn't help but urge him to hurry. After the rickshaw puller arrived at the back gate of Zhenjiang Customs and was paid the fare, he turned the rickshaw around and hadn't gone more than a few steps when he suddenly fell like a big tree in front of Xin Yi He store on Er Ma Road and died immediately. It is truly a case of valuing money over life.

Yangzhou

Notorious Bandit Zhi Xiaotao Executed: Zhi Xiaotao (also known as Zhi Xingkui), a notorious bandit from Yancheng, roamed the Jiangbei area, committing more than eighty cases of armed robbery, kidnapping, arson, and murder. Recently, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, based on complaints from victim Xiao Caiyou and others, dispatched special agents to Shanghai and captured him in the French Concession. He was extradited to Yangzhou a week ago. After interrogation by the Military Law Office of the Commissioner's Office, he confessed to various crimes and the plaintiff, Xiao Caiyou, was called to identify him as the perpetrator. On the morning of the 27th, at 10:00 AM, the Military Law Office brought him to court to verify his identity, tied him up, and took him to Kangshan execution ground where he was executed by shooting.

Xu the Tanner Kills His Three-Year-Old Sick Child by Throwing Him to the Ground: Xu the Tanner, who lives at the foot of the South City Wall of Xiaodongmen, because his three-year-old son was seriously ill, medical treatment was ineffective, and he was on the verge of death, was filled with extreme anger this day (the 27th). He grabbed his sick child from the room, threw him on the ground, and he died instantly. Those who heard about it cursed him for his ignorance and inhumanity.

Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Memorial Garden and Tomb of Martyr Xiong: The committee for preparing the construction of the Memorial Garden and Tomb of Martyr Xiong Chengji, initiated by Central Committee member Wang Boling, has now purchased more than ten mu of flat land on the east bank of the Dahong Bridge on the Slender West Lake in Yangzhou, as well as three to five small islands in the center of the lake, in preparation for building Weigen Park (Weigen is the martyr's courtesy name) and raising funds to repair and rebury the tomb of Qu Ji, which will be moved to Pingshan Hall in Yangzhou. Today (the 28th) at 10:00 AM, the groundbreaking ceremony was held. Chairman Wang Boling attended with group members. In addition to the representatives sent by the party and government agencies from the capital and provincial capitals, Zhang Zhijiang of the Pacification Commissioner's Office also personally attended and delivered a speech.

Pinghu

Mutinying Soldiers Reoccupy Xisi City: After the mutiny of the Sixteenth Company, Fourth Battalion, Seventh Regiment of the Provincial Security Force, they looted Xincang, Yamen Qian, Huxiao Bridge, Zhapu and several other towns, as already reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that after the encirclement and suppression, except for more than fifty who were captured alive, the rest all dispersed and fled to the sea. First, they gathered on Waipushan, an isolated island in the sea, and imprisoned all the monks in the mountain temple, restricting their movement. Then, they reorganized their ranks, boarded ships, and invaded Dushan in Xincang Town, and then penetrated further from Dushan and occupied Xisi City. At that time, Regiment Commander Shen Guocheng of the Seventh Regiment had arrived in Zhapu with troops from the province. After hearing the news, he left a platoon of soldiers to guard Zhapu and led the rest of his troops, as well as the county patrol team and a certain team from the Anti-Smuggling Battalion, to attack by land and water. On the outer sea, the Tai'an cruiser was intercepting them. A state of encirclement has now been formed, and the mutinying soldiers should not be difficult to eliminate in one fell swoop.

Bandit Liu Dexing Captured: Liu Dexing, a fierce and savage bandit under Taibao Ashu, was the champion among the bandits. Since the defeat of the gang, Liu Dexing continued to gather followers and cause trouble in Dongxiang. A few days ago, a self-surrendered bandit surnamed Chen reported to the 4th District Village Clearing Bureau. Upon receiving the report, Bureau Chief Gan Kaijun, together with the security team, searched the home of the Li family, where Liu Dexing was hiding. When they arrived at their destination, Liu Dexing and his men were already aware of it and ambushed in the forest, firing fiercely. A fierce battle ensued in the dark of night. By daybreak, the bandits had retreated, and Gan and his men searched forward. Suddenly, they saw Liu Dexing under a plum tree, panting like a cow. They immediately tied him up with ropes. Upon examining his body, they found that he had been shot through the chest and waist, each with one bullet hole. He was sent to the team headquarters. A document was prepared and submitted to the county government for reporting. The bandit lingered in the team headquarters until daybreak and then died. The county government sent Bureau Chief Xia of the Village Clearing Bureau to inspect him, photograph him, and record the case.

Hangzhou

Fuyang County Magistrate Transferred to Province and Reassigned: Yin Zhengyao, the County Magistrate of Fuyang, a native of Sheng County who passed the second county magistrate examination, has been in office for nearly four years. This month, he had a mutual assault with his wife, Qian Xiuyun. Ms. Qian came to the province to have her injuries examined by the court. Zhang Nanxian, the chairman of the Provincial Government, considered this matter to be related to the government's reputation and specifically proposed at the 411th Provincial Government meeting yesterday that Yin Zhengyao be transferred to the province and that Xu Erxin, a third-term county magistrate who is currently interning in the Department of Civil Affairs, be appointed to succeed him.

Case of Patrol Chief Accepting Bribes Transferred to Court: Wang Baosen, the patrol chief of the Xihu Manao Temple police post of the 6th Sub-bureau in the 2nd district of Hangzhou, and police officers Huang Hua and Zhang Bin, based on reports that there was gambling and opium smoking in the temple, Wang led the two police officers to apprehend them. They accepted a bribe of over eighty yuan on the spot and released the gamblers and opium smokers, dividing the money among themselves. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau found out about this matter and sent an inspector to investigate the temple. The money was handed over by the temple's tea boy, Li Changsheng, half in cash and half in checks. Over thirty yuan was also found in the patrol chief's bed. With the eyewitness accounts confirmed, the patrol chief, police officers, and the intermediary were all sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Yesterday, they were transferred to the Hangzhou District Court for interrogation.

City Water Will Be Fully Released: The city's tap water was previously scheduled to be

released on June 1st. Unexpectedly, since the beginning of summer, the weather has been rainy, and the opened water pipes and installation trenches have been flooded by water, making it impossible to work. Time has been delayed, so it cannot be completed as scheduled. They are currently working day and night to speed up the installation. It is estimated that if it does not rain too much, the installation and connection can be fully completed within July 20th. The water storage pool has been fully installed and equipped. The association plans to fully test the water in July and officially release the water from August 1st.

Verdict Announced Yesterday in the Case of Food Poisoning from Eggs and Rice: Song Deming and Jin Fuqing, employees of the Yuan Da Restaurant on Wushan Road, were accused of poisoning Ying Zhicheng, the ordnance adjutant of the Sixth Division. Yesterday, Judge Chen came to the criminal court to question the two defendants and immediately announced the verdict. Song Deming was sentenced to ten months in prison for the crime of business-related negligence causing injury to others. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be used to offset the sentence at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Jin Fuqing was found not guilty. The civil lawsuit attached to the plaintiff's case was transferred to the civil court for trial.

Son of Ge Qingyuan of Ningbo Kidnapped: In Xuanci Village near Yinjiang Bridge in Yinxian County, Ge Shuqing, a merchant, runs a winery for a living and is quite wealthy. The other night at about 8:00 PM, nine bandits suddenly arrived, armed with wooden cases, and intended to kidnap Ge Shuqing, but Ge was not there. The bandits then kidnapped Ge Qingyuan's twelve-year-old son, Nengye, who lived next door. Before leaving, they left a letter demanding 50,000 yuan and setting a deadline of 3:00 PM on the fourteenth day of the lunar month to meet with someone holding pine needles at the Dragon King Temple on Turtle Mountain, otherwise they would tear up the ticket and burn down the house. The victim has now reported the incident to the authorities for arrest and rescue.

Xiaoshan

Collision of Ships Results in Two Drownings: At Sanjiangkou on the night of the 27th, a paper cargo ship from Zhuji collided violently with a ferry heading to Zhuji, causing the boatmen to be unable to recover in time. Boatman Zhou Amao and his partner, Wei Xian, fell into the water and drowned. The next day, the ship went to Jianggan in Hangzhou to demand compensation from the paper cargo ship. It is unknown how this matter will be resolved.

Changes to the Method of Collecting Autonomous Household Donations: Last year, the township offices in Xiaoshan handled the autonomous household donations, and most of the money was controlled by the village chiefs and deputy chiefs, who either did not hand over the money or did not handle the matter at all, resulting in no funding for the district and county. The cleaners were sent to clean up for months, but there was no result. The fourth session of the County Administrative Meeting has now resolved that the township offices will collect the money themselves, turning over 25% to the county and district, with the rest used for the township office's recurring expenses. It is hoped that this method may have some effect.

Anqing

The Tianchang County Anti-Party Case Expands: The Tianchang County Anti-Party case occurred in Anhui on June 8th. Because the idols in the county's City God Temple had been destroyed earlier, the masses requested their restoration. The county magistrate entrusted the matter to the county party headquarters. As a result, the masses destroyed the party headquarters three times and demolished the private residence of Party Secretary Zhang Qingcheng. The provincial party headquarters sent personnel to investigate, but there is still no concrete solution. The county's various sectors have specially formed a six-member Anti-Party Support Association, which is attacking the county magistrate, Wu Shuxun.

Changes to the Method of Collecting License Fees: The Anhui Department of Civil Affairs submitted a request to the provincial government to make slight changes to the method of collecting license fees by the Shipping Administration. The provincial government has approved the record. The method of license registration was originally fixed for four periods each year: January 1st to the end of March for the first period, April 1st to the end of June for the second period, July 1st to the end of September for the third period, and October 1st to the end of December for the fourth period. Now, those who wish to pay in full at once will be charged 80%, and those who pay twice will be charged 90%. Those who still pay four times are also free to do so, but they cannot ask for a discount.

Dispute over the Use of Temple Property for Education in Hao County: The Hao County Education Bureau previously requested the Buddhist Association to donate 5,000 yuan annually from the income of the temple property for education expenses. This case has been in dispute for three years and has not been resolved. Yesterday, the Department of Civil Affairs received an order from the province to thoroughly investigate and report on this case, and specifically ordered the county magistrate to create a detailed register of the county's isolated temples, wild temples, and the amount of temple property, and report it to the department for resolution.

Letter to the Editor

Letter from the Zhenhai County Government 69

Dear Editor,

I have read your newspaper's Ningbo News on the 25th, which contained an item about the suspension of the Zhenhai County Magistrate for investigation. It stated that Zhenhai County Magistrate Cao Boquan was accused by the people of dereliction of duty and accepting bribes, and the provincial government secretly ordered his detention for investigation. The content is quite inconsistent with the facts. The reason for County Magistrate Cao's suspension this time, according to the central government's order, is only due to suspected negligence, not dereliction of duty or acceptance of bribes. I am writing a special letter to request a correction to clarify the facts.

Sincerely, Zhenhai County Government

Political Platform of the Chinese Nationalist Party 70

Article 6 of Domestic Policy: Affirm the people's complete freedom of assembly, association, discussion, publication, residence, and belief.

Article 4 of Domestic Policy: Implement universal suffrage and abolish class elections based on property as the standard.

Articles 7 and 8 of Domestic Policy: Strictly set the legal amount of land tax and prohibit all extra levies such as likin, which should all be abolished.

Article 12 of Domestic Policy: Affirm in law, economy, education, and society the principle of equality between men and women and promote the development of women's rights.

Article 9 of Domestic Policy: Investigate the population, organize arable land, and adjust the production and sales of grain to ensure that the people have sufficient food.

Director of the Hunan Education Department Huang Shiheng Requests Resignation 72

Due to the Shortage of Education Funding

Huang Shiheng, the Director of the Hunan Education Department, submitted a request to the Executive Yuan of the National Government and the Ministry of Education for his resignation, and also requested an additional allocation of 100,000 yuan for education funding. The original submission is as follows: "For the sake of insufficient funds and inability to maintain, earnestly request to resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. It is hoped that your consideration will be granted. I humbly believe that education is the foundation of the nation, and funding is the lifeline of education. The education funding of Hunan Province has been repeatedly requested to implement an additional salt tax of one yuan and five jiao to complete the province's independent education funding for more than two years. Written communications and representatives' petitions have not stopped to this day. Exhausted and hoarse, they have only managed to retain the original education surcharge of eight jiao per package, which has been converted from unified salt tax collection and supplemented by the national treasury at 93,100 yuan per month, losing the original spirit of independence. The education sector believes that the salt tax surcharge comes from the special burden of the people of Hunan. It has been approved by your office to add one yuan and five jiao, but it has not been implemented, causing teachers to blame the education administration for ineffective work. Even from the perspective of self-examination, it is difficult to justify myself. This is one reason why I cannot but resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. Education bureaus in various counties and joint county-run and private schools have historically collected education funds from the likin tax, totaling more than 170,000 yuan per year in Changsha and other counties. After the abolition of the likin tax, this additional collection of funds is completely unavailable. Although the meeting of your office has a resolution to allocate and compensate from the local national tax revenue, it has also been appealed through written communications and representatives' petitions, but it is ultimately a hollow benefit that does not reach the schools. The schools in each county are actually unable to maintain themselves, and they cannot help but be blamed. This is a second reason why I cannot but resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. The minimum monthly funding required for provincial schools and private school subsidies in Hunan Province is more than 180,000 yuan, not including temporary expenses. Although the budget for mass education funding has been listed at 400,000 yuan for many years, only a portion has been spent in the 18th year of the Republic. In addition, the funding for compulsory education has not been actively raised. Before the abolition of the likin tax, the monthly deficit was fully paid by the provincial treasury. After the abolition of the likin tax, the provincial treasury is strained, and all government expenses still depend on the central government's subsidy of 200,000 yuan. The funding for provincial schools and private school subsidies is only allocated at 50% per month, and the remaining 50% is completely empty and unavailable. How can this be sustained if it accumulates month after month and year after year? This is a third reason why I cannot but resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. During the period of political tutelage, the popularization of education is particularly important. If we want to achieve popularization, we must implement compulsory education without delay. The regulations for the implementation of compulsory education in Hunan Province, the source of funds for which is to be obtained from temple and ancestral hall properties, surcharges on land taxes, surcharges on tobacco and alcohol, and donations from wealthy people, were mostly determined ten years ago. Now there is no way to find them. Recently, the supervision and restrictions on temple and ancestral hall properties have been strengthened, and tobacco and alcohol have been turned over to national taxation, and the surcharges have been abolished accordingly. The counties and districts have no other way to raise funds for compulsory education except to add surcharges to land taxes or mu donations. In recent years, there have been many local changes, such as the organization of local defense volunteer teams and all new policies, all of which depend on land tax surcharges. Some have increased from one tael of regular tax to more than ten yuan or even twenty yuan. It is really unbearable to add more levies and increase the burden on the people. The local compulsory education is unable to be carried out, and it is also true that they are often exhausted in responding to requests to increase land taxes or mu donations for compulsory education funds. This is a fourth reason why I cannot but resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. Previously, the request to resign was actually due to the difficulty in obtaining education funds. It has been delayed for several months without being approved. I had no choice but to return to my post in accordance with the instructions, and I also stated that it would be limited to two months. Now, it has been nearly five months since I returned to my post, and there is even less of a solution to the education funding situation compared to before. Even the administrative expenses of the department are five months in arrears, and I am really unable to continue to support it. This is the fifth reason why I cannot but resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. I humbly observe that the education funds in Anhui Province have historically been provided by paper and tobacco donations and likin taxes. Since paper and tobacco have been turned over to national taxation, the central government has subsidized several million yuan. After the abolition of the likin tax, the education funds in Anhui Province are subsidized by the national treasury at 150,000 yuan per month. I have heard that the education funds in Fujian Province are also subsidized by the central government at more than 10,000 yuan per month. The education funds in Hunan Province are obtained from surcharges on toiletries, which are specially borne by the people of Hunan. Even if the surcharges are fully allocated to education funds, it is a legitimate demand of the people of Hunan. Now, due to the unified salt tax collection, the future of education in Hunan Province should be considered. Following the examples of Anhui and Fujian, in addition to verifying the original 93,100 yuan, the national treasury should provide at least an additional 100,000 yuan per month to offset the deficit. Otherwise, if they are all under the same protection and are affected by the unified financial system, they will inevitably be unevenly distributed, and I feel even more ashamed. This is the sixth reason why I cannot but resign from all current and concurrent positions to avoid causing delays. I, Shiheng, am grateful for the knowledge and encounters, and have served as the Director of the Hunan Education Department for more than two years. I am ashamed that I have made no achievements and have failed to live up to your wise judgment of people. Before the rebellion last year, all plans could be gradually implemented. After the rebellion, there were many holes and flaws, and the implementation of the abolition of the likin tax was extremely difficult. Maintaining the status quo has exhausted my energy. If I simply follow the routine and waste resources, I will not only bear the name of holding a position without performing my duties, but also go against the government's principle of seeking truth from facts. I earnestly hope that you will consider my sincere feelings, approve my resignation from all current and concurrent positions, and allow me to rest for a while, so that I may be able to make contributions in the future. However, education is an extremely active undertaking, and it must not be interrupted due to the resignation of Shiheng alone. I still hope that you will uphold the President's legacy of increasing education funding and protecting its independence, and implement the original proposal to approve an additional surcharge of one yuan and five jiao on salt taxes, and approve the national treasury to allocate an additional 100,000 yuan per month, so that education in Hunan Province can continue to progress, which I would gratefully experience. All the reasons for the request to resign and the approval of additional education funding are urgently presented to your judgment for consideration. I am extremely frightened and await your orders."

District Nine Counties Elementary School Summer Lecture Meeting 73

Education Department Dispatches Personnel to Organize Committee

In the past, all counties in Jiangsu Province held summer lecture meetings for elementary school teachers during the summer vacation. Previously, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education had formulated regulations for handling these meetings and ordered their implementation. This year, Chen Hexian, the director of the Department of Education, felt that holding these events separately in each county led to issues of unconcentrated talent and financial resources, hindering significant results. Furthermore, Jiangpu, Liuhe, and other counties submitted requests to jointly organize the lectures across several counties. Consequently, the department carefully considered the matter and established provisional measures for setting up regional summer lecture meetings for elementary school teachers, as well as an organizational outline for the summer lecture meeting committee. The entire province was divided into six districts, with the fourth district comprising nine counties: Tongzhou, Rugao, Haimen, Yancheng, Funing, Dongtai, Taixian, Taixing, and Qidong. The lecture meeting was to be held in Nantong, combining the talents and financial resources of the nine counties to manage it. Chen Haicheng, the principal of Nantong Middle School, was appointed as the director. In addition, the directors of the education bureaus of the nine counties and the principal of Nantong Middle School, totaling ten individuals, were organized into the district committee. The Department of Education specially dispatched a committee member to serve as the chairman of the committee, planning all aspects of the summer lecture meeting, such as reviewing the budget, hiring lecturers, and determining subjects and class hours. All matters were to be overseen by the committee. It is reported that Yao Hechu, a secretary from the Department of Education, has been designated as the chairman of the committee and will arrive in Nantong soon. The first committee meeting is scheduled for July 1st. Extracurricular lecturers have also been engaged, including prominent figures in education such as Yang Xingfo, Wang Maozu, and Zhu Lu.

Suzhou Zhenhua Girls' School Graduation Ceremony 74

Suzhou Private Zhenhua Girls' Middle School held its graduation ceremony yesterday (the 27th). There were approximately 120 graduates from the senior high, junior high, and elementary school levels. Around 300 to 400 family members and guests attended the event. The meeting commenced as scheduled, followed by the principal's report on administrative and financial matters. The paths of past graduates were divided into two categories: further education and service. Those pursuing further education accounted for 70% to 80%, mostly entering universities such as Central University, Tsinghua University, Yenching University, Ginling College, Soochow University, and the University of Shanghai. Those in service were generally competent and enjoyed their work. Afterward, prominent figures delivered speeches. Mu Ouchu's address was titled "The Responsibilities of Women in the Future," emphasizing three aspects: engaging in education, promoting its expansion, and advocating for its advancement. Xu Shuzhao, the director of the Business School at Central University, and representatives from various sectors, including the director of moral education, Yu Qingtang, also delivered speeches. Due to length constraints, they were omitted. In the afternoon, a school council was held, with Chairman Yu Qingtang reporting on the construction of the new library and discussing preparations for the 25th anniversary celebration in the upcoming semester. Furthermore, Wang Jiyi, the former director of affairs at the school and a master's degree holder, recently returned from the United States after studying education and has rejoined the faculty. It is expected that he will bring about improvements soon, which is certainly anticipated.

Chinese Tennis Club Doubles Finals Tomorrow 79

Yesterday's Semi-Final Results

Guo Zhan and Yu Liu Groups Win

Competing for the Championship Tomorrow

The Chinese Tennis Club's Open Doubles Tennis Tournament, held over one to two weeks, eliminated weaker teams. Yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM, the semi-finals were held. As a result, Dun Qida and Zhan Wanyao's team defeated Qian Yaobin and Feng Nianci's team 3-1, and Yu Tianguang and Liu Keng's team defeated Wang Hong and Sun Chengbi's team 3-1. Tomorrow, Guo Zhan and Yu Liu will compete for the championship.

Guo Zhan Defeats Qian Feng

Guo Qida and Zhan Wanyao {6-3, 6-4, 6-3, 6-1} Qian Yaobin and Feng Nianci

Guo Zhan defeated Qian Feng 3-1. The difference in skill was clear. Qian and Feng were too agitated, often touching the net and missing shots. They also showed signs of arguing with each other. When impatient, their shots were inaccurate. Guo Qida, on the other hand, was calm and extraordinary. After losing the first set 3-6, Guo Ning exerted great effort in the second set, leading 3-2, then 4-3, and then 5-4, finally winning the set 6-4. In the second and third sets, Qian Feng steadily declined and lacked defensive strength.

Yu Liu Defeats Wang Sun

Yu Tianguang and Liu Keng {6-3, 9-7, 3-6, 6-1} Wang Hong and Sun Chengbi

The pairing of these two groups was not ideal. Liu was inferior to Yu, and Sun was inferior to Wang. Liu Keng made too many mistakes, unable to get even steady balls over the net. His smash into the net was accurate. Yu Tianguang was also less steady than before. Among the four, he was the best, with effective serves and decent smashes. His forehand and backhand shots were impressive. Wang Hong could be considered satisfactory, but Sun Chengbi was weaker. Yu Liu's victory in the second set was hard-won. After leading 5-3, they lost three consecutive games, falling behind 6-7. However, they worked hard to regain three games and win. Wang and the others won the third set, but the fourth set was a crushing defeat, ending their hopes.

Grass Tennis Club A and B Group League 80

Scheduled to Begin on July 8th

Chinese Tennis Club Participates in A Group

The Shanghai Westerners' Grass Tennis Club's A and B Group Tennis League is scheduled to begin on July 8th. This year's participation is crowded, with eleven teams in Group A and eleven teams in Group B, listed below.

Group A Teams: Shanghai General Association, French Business Association, Rax, Portugal, Japan Tennis Club, YMCA, American Country Club, Xieqiao General Association, Western Police Team, Chinese Tennis Club, Japan Ocean Company.

Group B Teams: Shanghai General Association, French Business Association, Portugal, Japan Tennis Club, YMCA, Western Police Team, German Garden General Association, Swiss Tennis Club, Waterworks Tennis Club, British-American Tobacco Tennis Club.

Competition Dates: As in previous years, the competition will begin on the first Friday of July. Last year, it was changed to Wednesday, which was deemed more convenient, so this year it will also be held every Wednesday. However, since the first Wednesday of July is the 1st, it will be postponed to the 8th. The competition must be completed within three days.

Venue Issues: The Grass Club is seriously considering the venue. The Racecourse Courts will no longer be available after September 15th, so all those who use the Racecourse as their home ground will hold events earlier, prioritizing avoiding conflicts.

Team Composition: The Japanese team requested to join with two teams this year, but due to overcrowding, it will have to be postponed to next year. Some members of the YMCA team last year were members of other teams. The Xieqiao General Association only has one team joining Group A. New entrants include the Western Police Team, YMCA team, and Chinese Association. The Chinese Association has participated before.

Municipal First Stadium Amateur Basketball Elite Group Championship 84

Belongs to the Nanxing Team

The Municipal First Stadium Amateur Basketball Competition's elite group round-robin results showed that the Nanxing, Sheguang, and Heixing teams formed a three-way tie. After the elimination matches, Heixing initially gained the final victory without any effort due to the Nanxing team's insufficient number of players and Sheguang's withdrawal. Now, it has been discovered that a certain player in the Heixing team is a school student, which is inconsistent with Article 3 of the association's charter. The team's qualifications should be cancelled, and all competition results should be invalidated. Furthermore, during the round-robin matches, Nanxing lost once to Heixing. Now that Heixing's qualifications have been cancelled, Nanxing has regained its winning position and indeed won this year's elite group championship.

Jiangnan Track and Field Team Tries Out in Beijing 85

Wang Jihuai | Javelin 47.60 Meters

| Breaks National Record |

Nanjing, 28th - The Jiangnan track and field team went to Beijing early in the morning of the 26th, transferred by train to the north. Yesterday, they performed practice at the track and field field of Central University in Beijing, from 4:00 PM to 7:20 PM. Central University students also participated in the practice. Wang Jihuai's javelin throw reached 47.60 meters, breaking the national record, truly adding glory to the entire army. Ma Fengrui's 10,000-meter race was a lone wolf chase with no one to compete with, but the weather was very hot, and he stopped halfway. Cao Yu's pole vault was a solo performance, reaching 3.15 meters, but it was too dark to continue. In total, out of thirteen events, Jiangnan held the top spot in ten events. In the 800-meter race, Central University's Zhou Minzhang was first, with a time of 2 minutes 13 seconds. In the 1,500-meter race, Cao Chengjin won first place with a time of 4 minutes 37 seconds. Cao was formerly a representative from Hebei and is now employed at Central University. In the discus throw, Central University's Gao Shangzhi was first with 31.32 meters. After the performance, Central University specially prepared a grand banquet to entertain the team that evening. This morning, they crossed the river northwards.

Tension in the World Tennis Championships Singles 86

Only Eight Men and Women Remain | Borotra Flew Back from France

London, 27th - Thousands of fans at the Wimbledon Tennis Championships today were eager to know who the last eight men and women in the singles competition would be. The atmosphere was incredibly tense.

Last Eight Men's Singles Players

The order of the final eight, as drawn, is as follows:

Austin (England) vs. Shields (USA)

Wood (USA) vs. Hughes (England)

Bury (England) vs. Van Ryn (USA)

Sato Jiro (Japan) vs. Borotra (France)

Borotra Flew Back from France

The King and Queen of England attended the matches today. The spectators were extremely crowded, and the sun shone brightly. France's Borotra flew back from France today and defeated Austria's Artl directly in three sets. His performance was excellent, and the King and Queen greatly praised him.

Sato Jiro's Masterpiece

Japan's Sato Jiro greatly defeated England's Lee today, which was surprising. He suffered a slight setback at the beginning, but the results were 8-6, 6-4, 6-3. It took Sato a long time to gain momentum. Lee had taken a 4-1 lead in the first set, but Sato won four consecutive games, or 5-5. Although Lee made it 6-6 again, Sato won two more games. In the last two games, Sato's extremely angled shots were incredibly accurate, and he scored points almost every time. His serves were not particularly impressive. In the semi-finals, Sato will face Borotra.

Austin to Meet Shields

Austin defeated Collins 6-3, 6-3, 6-4 very easily. In the semi-finals, he will face the "dark horse" American Shields.

Last Eight Women's Singles Players

The last eight women's singles players are: (1) Miss Olsen (Germany), (2) Madame Paniautoff (Switzerland), (3) Madame Mathieu (France), (4) Miss Scriven (England), (5) Miss Nuttall (England), (6) Miss Helen Jacobs (USA), (7) Miss Krawinkel (Germany), (8) Miss Lunnert (England)

Junior Championships Defeat Strong Opponents

In the junior championships, Miss Scriven defeated Miss Letley 6-1, 6-4 very easily. Miss Scriven has defeated a succession of strong opponents, such as Madame Shegetoff, a Belgian champion, Miss Harvard, a Grey Trott Cup player from the USA, and Miss Shire of Central Europe.

Miss Helen to Meet a Formidable Opponent

Mrs. Goffrey was defeated by the American Helen Jacobs 6-2, 6-1, which was unexpected. Mrs. Goffrey's performance was far from what it was when she won the titles in 1924 and 1926. She had a smooth start, with strong net play and smashes, which left her opponent almost exhausted. However, she gradually lost her touch with her forehand shots, and her opponent aggressively attacked with backhand shots. Miss Jacobs' serves were very powerful. In the semi-finals, she will face the formidable Miss Nuttall.

Mrs. Harper Submits Again

Miss Nuttall had defeated Mrs. Harper of the United States 6-4, 6-2 last year to win the All-American title. Today, she defeated her again. In the first set, Nuttall made many mistakes, possibly because she was too eager to win. Her serves were poor, but her shots were powerful. Mrs. Harper had a 3-1 lead in the first set, but Nuttall gradually gained momentum, making it 4-4. Nuttall's shots were heavy and powerful, and Harper often touched the ball after it bounced and failed to return it. Nuttall's serves after the bounce were particularly good.

Mrs. Van Ryn Lost to the Frenchwoman

Mrs. Van Ryn of the United States lost to Madame Mathieu of France 6-4, 6-3.
