Free Talk

Eastern Scale and Western Claw 87

— Qiu Shui

Australia consumes chocolate worth seven million pounds annually. The chocolate factories employ tens of thousands of people. Even literary figures and artists with social standing are recruited to design chocolate trademarks, names, leaflets, and packaging methods.

Recently, a French scientist invented artificial fog. Within an hour, he can use chemical methods to create fog over a specific area of two square miles.

More than five thousand cars enter London daily.

The United States has the most developed construction industry. The number of 洋房 (Western-style houses) with more than twenty floors is 377, and half of them are located in New York City.

Trains are the safest means of transportation. According to recent statistics, only one person dies in every 56.8 million train journeys.

British airplane pilots receive extremely high salaries. London has 320 pilots, most of whom earn an annual salary of one thousand pounds.

In the United Kingdom, only 3.5 out of every 100 people own a telephone. In the United States, 12 out of every 100 people own a telephone.

A Brief Note on the New Jing'an Temple 88

— Wang Yanjin

After class on Tuesday, I went to Shanghai for some business. Guongan said to me, "You didn't have time to visit Jing'an Temple during the Buddha's Birthday. Can we go together tonight to fulfill your long-cherished wish?" I agreed. After completing my errands, I bought a train ticket and went, returning after 9 o'clock when I had had my fill. This is a brief record of my fleeting impressions, leaving a small trace.

A Grand Elementary School - When I visited in the past, the desks and chairs were scattered and in disarray, revealing an untidy and unclean state. Now, the new building is complete, and the schoolhouse is brand new. Principal Wu led the tour, from the chapel to the dormitory, all neatly arranged, making people envious. Guongan left me with Principal Wu to discuss elementary school education. We talked to each other, counting off educational experiences like family treasures. When we parted, the school's administrative officer handed me a piece of paper, asking me to add criticism. I really didn't dare to comment, so I briefly wrote that Jing'an Elementary School has already achieved remarkable results since its founding, but it hasn't paid enough attention to sports. I hope it will focus on rectifying this after the summer vacation, etc. This is a truthful record; how could I dare to make reckless slander or praise?

A Quiet and Simple Buddhist Hall - Jing'an Temple is the only ancient temple in Shanghai. Since the monk Zhifa has been in charge, he has undertaken reforms in every aspect. He has rebuilt collapsed parts and repaired damaged parts. The Buddhist hall, in particular, is extremely quiet and simple, with a momentum that rivals the dragon's transformation on the South China Sea coast. In the transportation hub of this concession, an ancient temple still stands alone in its quietness. The phrase "a Peach Blossom Spring in a secular world" can almost be used to describe it. I regret that my character is foolish and vulgar, and I have no inclination to cultivate myself. Otherwise, entering the temple to practice and become a Buddha would surely be a pleasant thing.

A Seat Bathed in Buddhist Light - Zhifa has a deep understanding of Buddhism. Seeing the fickleness of the world today, he has gathered famous scholars such as Wang Yiheng, Jiang Baiqi, and Wang Dun'gen to form the Buddhist Light Society, so as to promote the light of Buddhism and save people's hearts. Tonight, he specially hosted the press, and over fifty guests gathered. A simple vegetarian meal was served, and the entire room was bathed in Buddhist light, making it a grand occasion.

Anecdotes of General Feng Yipei 89

— Yan Xifeng

General Yipei, a native of Xinhui, Guangdong, graduated from the Baoding Military Academy. After the National Revolutionary Army pacified Nanjing, he successively served as the deputy commander of the military officer corps, director of the training corps preparatory office, commander of the first training division, and commander of the National Government Guard Division. Recently, he was ordered by the central government to be the commander of the National Government Guard Army. He recently suffered from appendicitis and was admitted to the Central Hospital, but he died of septicemia at 2 PM on the 24th, a great loss to the central government. During his lifetime, Feng was honest and diligent. Last year, he made great contributions to the campaign against Yan and Feng. Before the commander-in-chief went to Jiangxi, he originally intended to lead the team there, but he died suddenly in these past few days. All the officers and soldiers of the entire division were in tears. Tomorrow, the coffin will be moved to the Liangguang Guildhall. All officers above the rank of major in the entire army must go to the funeral.

Feng was quite fat and often wore tortoiseshell-framed glasses. His military uniform and leather boots were always spotless. Once, he went to inspect the second infantry regiment, and one of the buttons on his chest was unbuttoned. The gatekeeper buttoned it up for him. After returning to the headquarters, he issued an order to reward the soldier and gave him ten silver dollars. He often gave speeches on the memorial platform, saying, "I hope the officers and soldiers of this division will pay attention to exercise and not imitate the corpulence of your division commander." After saying this, he would laugh softly. Feng also urged the officers and soldiers to be thrifty because the cost of living in Beijing was high, saying that young people are most likely to fall into the trap of love. "You should remember the many difficulties of the party and the country, endure hardship and be self-restrained." He was extremely meticulous in encouraging those who came after him. He was fair in financial matters and in employing people. He often said that he did not want to become a warlord. All the officers were recommended and commissioned by the commander-in-chief. He, as the division commander, had never recommended a single person. In fact, there were many of his old subordinates. Compared to the so-called big shots, his personality was dozens of times higher. Feng also had an old mother at home, to whom he was an extremely filial son. He often said that when he was a platoon leader, his monthly income was thirty yuan, of which he used twenty yuan to support his mother and ten yuan for himself. At this time, when the country is in turmoil and morality is collapsing, he passed away. Observers mourn and regret his passing. When he set out last year, he gathered all the officers and soldiers and said, "The officers and soldiers of the training division are not allowed to be defeated." His heroic spirit could be imagined. After setting out, he successively captured the important towns of Longhai, Mamuji, and Guide. Since then, he drove straight into Ji and fought in western Henan. He was always present in every battle and won every battle. After returning to Beijing in triumph, he continued training as usual, without the slightest arrogance. Heaven did not grant him many years. It is truly lamentable. Now, I will write a few words based on what I know to express my condolences.

Returning After Watching "Chai Tou Feng" 90

— Cao Mengyu

The play "Chai Tou Feng" is Hui Sheng's only masterpiece. Its popularity is largely due to Lu You's story, which has a literary and historical connection. My friend Lin Ziliqin also came to Shanghai from afar for this reason. On the twenty-third night, Hui Sheng performed this play. I invited Ziliqin to watch it. However, I was late because I went to a banquet, arriving at ten o'clock. Ju Peng's performance of "The Prime of Spring and Autumn" had already reached the "Zhaoguan" scene, and I was unable to fully enjoy the clear and melodious performance.

Hui Sheng has a unique understanding of this play, so his singing, acting, and recitations are all perfected. His skill is beyond words. In a word, it is truly beautiful and good. The conception of this play is excellent, reaching the peak of perfection. Although it is not entirely in line with official history, this is where its strength lies. The economy of the writing is like the paintings of the New Luo Eight Masters, with few strokes but a distinct style. The layout is particularly clever, interweaving the stories of romantic heroes, with everything secretly echoing each other. Just as Song Shiheng and Dugu Ce have chivalry, Lu You and Tang Huixian have infatuation. There is also Lu's mother's violence and Bukong's lechery. As for the scene of writing the poem in Shen Garden, from the perspective of ordinary people's compassion, it seems inappropriate for Shiheng to use a deceptive trick to test Fangweng by having Dugu Ce falsely say that Huixian is Shiheng's new favorite, causing Fangweng to write the heartbreaking poem and causing Huixian to read the poem and grieve greatly, resulting in a tragic situation. Although the matter is cruel and loses the constant hope of the circle being complete, if this section is deleted, the spirit of the entire play will be scattered, and there will be no room for people to chew on. Moreover, the day that Huixian died, the day that she returned to Fangweng, the music passing through the venue was enough to express the roundness of the wedding night, giving people a satisfaction that is not completely satisfying. This kind of wonderful point is like Nan Gong's calligraphy, where the meaning arrives but the pen does not. Otherwise, a flat narrative without any surprising strokes would also be of value. As for the tightness of the stage and the touching nature of the plot, it is felt that it becomes more and more urgent. At that time, there were three or five women sitting nearby who exclaimed in surprise whenever they saw a tragic scene. Alas, the sound and color moved people to such an extent. Although Ziliqin is not a woman, he was also moved and sighed repeatedly. After returning, he wrote a poem to show me: "The death is tragic, the life is sad, so many strange things / There is no medicine to cure the infatuation of love / A heartbroken 'Chai Tou Feng' / Is left for Xunlang to compose bamboo branches." / The moon is dim, the lights are faint, and the night is late / Sad strings compose heart-wrenching words / How can one bear to hear the cuckoo cry and the wild geese scream / Tears wet my green shirt without my knowing.

Experience Talk on Treating Consumption 91

— He Tieshan

Using medicine to treat illness is no different from using soldiers to quell rebellion. One must employ both suppression and appeasement to succeed. This is especially true for treating consumption. Because the fundamental vitality is already damaged, it is like a weak country facing internal rebellion and forced to use military force. While simultaneously suppressing and appeasing, one should pay attention to national planning and the people's livelihood. If the foundation of the country is stable, the rebellion will be easily quelled. Our country's doctors have always known the difficulty of treating consumption with medicine. However, they often disdain to inquire about the new anti-consumption drugs on the market and rely solely on one or two ancient formulas, adding and subtracting superficially. How can one expect them to be effective? Since I hung my gourd (began practicing medicine) in Shanghai thirty years ago, I have always been interested in researching both Chinese and Western new drugs. I am happy to publicize those that are beneficial and can aid in treatment. Recently, I tried Yijin Grass, produced by the Peisheng Pharmaceutical Company at 203 Zhonghua Road in this city, and the results were excellent. Its nature is mild and its effects are rapid. It is truly a good medicine for eradicating lung disease. To use a military analogy, it is the army of a strong country pacifying internal rebellion. Therefore, I record a few words as a report after my experimentation.

Art News: Mr. Zhang Zhenlu, a novelist and calligrapher, has recently collaborated with the old painter Mr. Ma Henian on fan paintings. One is in cursive script and the other is a green landscape. They will be on display starting today at the Liangchen Haoyou Society on Beijing Road near Touji Bridge, for ten days. During the exhibition, each fan painting will be sold for two yuan. Mail orders are also accepted from other cities. If a large quantity is needed for awards, they can be made to order quickly at a reduced price during the exhibition period. (Art Shùnmín)

Indian Travelogue (56) 92

— Linghua

On the morning of the 22nd, I returned to Varanasi. In the car, I met a professor who talked about the superstition of the Indian caste system. He said that the so-called caste system is not just divided into first, second, third, and fourth classes. Each class is further divided into several levels. Even Islam is the same. Generally, each class is divided into ten factions. Each faction does not interact with each other and cannot marry. He listed an example for me. Each class has its own specialized term. All Indians can be divided into hundreds of thousands of classes, never interacting with each other and never having the hope of cooperation. This is why it is always difficult to obtain freedom. Moreover, the languages and writing systems are different in each province, so English is more commonly used. All these obstacles give others good opportunities. Therefore, Indian freedom is not easy to achieve. On the way, I saw wheat ripening. Men and women were harvesting wheat in the fields. Recalling the wealthy in the city chasing the wind in their cars, when can equality be discussed? Furthermore, the Indian movement is different from the Chinese movement. All Indian movements have a leader, and the activists are very different from the free movement of Chinese youths. I thought that the Indian caste system is so strict that there is no possibility of movement. They want their people to be like salted fish, never active. However, there are signs that it is becoming difficult to maintain. The new tide is rising daily. In the future, the caste system will eventually be eliminated.

In the afternoon, I arrived in Varanasi and stayed at the Indian school.

On the morning of the 23rd, at dawn, I heard the students' prayer songs. It is their daily ritual. Indians are so fond of gods that their children are well-behaved and respectful. Everywhere I went, I often saw young people bowing to me. Those who bowed included students and laborers. The laboring class bows to the master class as a matter of course. Even very young children, only three or four years old, know to bow when they see a guest. How fond Indians are of goodness! When I traveled in Japan, everyone was polite. Only the Chinese, who claim to be the land of ritual and music, are also very arrogant. Everywhere they go, they often cheat foreigners. Even people from one province cheat people from another province. I hope educators pay close attention to this. A servant showed me the three threads he wore on his body, saying they were very important. I asked what they meant. He replied that the three threads indicate which god he belongs to, what his surname is, and what his class is. These three threads are closely related to the three hairs on his head. Only now did I realize why Indians keep a few hairs on their heads. It is to indicate their class and lineage. It is not easy for foreigners to investigate. There are things that I do not pay attention to, but they consider very important. This is the case.

Rotary Club

??? (6) 93

— Xu Zhuodai

The wife, without a word, really went downstairs. Ziliang was entangled by her and felt very confused, and he was also hungry. It was not easy for him to start writing for a while. He simply closed his eyes and rested his mind, planning to calm down before he could work. Unexpectedly, after a short rest, there was a loud noise on the stairs, and the wife came up. She strode into the pavilion, holding a pencil in one hand and a piece of white paper in the other, standing next to the desk:

"My composition is finished, correct it for me first!"

Saying that, she put the white paper in front of Ziliang. When Ziliang looked at the title, he didn't understand:

"What is this title?"

"Old Uncle Wang's virgin death. That is to say, it is his first time dying."

"What are you talking about?"

"Chinese!"

Ziliang didn't look closely at her article and threw it into the wastepaper basket next to him. When the wife saw it, she sat down on a couple of chairs with her body and covered her face with her hands, crying. At first, Ziliang was very calm, no matter what she did, he didn't say a word. Later, he thought that his disposal seemed a bit excessive. When he looked at her again, she was still crying, her shoulders moving violently. Ziliang thought: If she keeps crying, I certainly can't work. It's better to coax her downstairs, so he walked over and patted her on the shoulder:

"Stop crying! It's my fault."

Unexpectedly, before Ziliang finished speaking, the wife suddenly took her hands away from her face and laughed loudly. Where were the tears on her face? Ziliang was dumbfounded at this moment.

"This afternoon, I'm going to the swimming pool alone. I don't need you to take me."

"In a couple of days, I will take you. You can't go alone!" Mrs. Yueru stood up:

"Why can't I go? Are you afraid that I will run away with another man? To be honest, I have always been well-behaved. In the first grade of elementary school, there were boys and girls in the same class. Only you Pan family women are very unruly!"

Ziliang felt strange:

"Pan family women are unruly? In our family? Who?"

"Your ancestors produced several licentious women:"

"Bullshit!"

Ziliang sat back in his original seat.

"Your seventeenth or eighteenth generation great-aunt Pan Jinlian and Pan Qiaoyun were not good people!"

"Nonsense!"

Local News

China Merchant Mariners' Association Requests Retrieval of Pilotage Rights 94

Foreigners' Conspiracy to Continue Monopoly on Selection

National Rights and National Defense Should be Made Permanent

The China Merchant Mariners' Association submitted a petition to the three ministries of the Ministry of Maritime Transport, Communications, and Finance, stating: "The petition is to request, based on the resolutions of the National Congress and the spirit of abolishing unequal treaties, to promptly issue an order stipulating that pilots in all Chinese ports should be appointed by Chinese nationals, and to set a time limit for the retrieval of pilotage powers currently occupied by foreigners in various ports, in order to strengthen national rights and consolidate national defense. Whether the military defense security of a country's ports is secure is closely related to the nationality of the pilots. No matter how meticulously the port defenses are arranged, they cannot be completely sealed off during wartime, and there must be a navigable route. If the pilots are not nationals of the country, the enemy can easily buy them off, so that once Chen Cang is secretly crossed, even if there is a natural barrier, it is as if it does not exist. This is why all countries in the world attach great importance to the fact that, except for those ports unrelated to national defense where pilots are not always stationed, all pilots must be nationals of the country. In our country, in the Jia Shen Sino-French Battle of Ma Jiang, and the Boxer Allied Forces Battle of Dagu, foreign nationals served as pilots, leading the enemy deep into our territory, and our army was defeated, resulting in a heavy alliance under the city. The Chinese people have not forgotten, and all those with blood and qi, recalling the past, who would not be heartbroken and weep? Therefore, since the establishment of the revolutionary government, from the government to the people, regarding navigation rights that affect the national economy and people's livelihood, and pilots who are related to national defense security, all know that the ignorance and arbitrariness of the previous Qing Dynasty in losing sovereignty was an unconscious act of treason, and advocate the unconditional retrieval as soon as possible. Although it has not yet been realized, it can be said that it is in the process of brewing and proceeding. Therefore, the association has also loudly appealed for the retrieval of navigation rights and submitted detailed proposals again and again. Recently, there has been the organization of the National Pilots Association, all with the aim of retrieving the lost national rights as soon as possible, completing the actual independence of the country, and fulfilling the duty of a national. Recently, foreigners from non-treaty countries have learned definite news that foreign pilots in Shanghai and other places, knowing that the association is making the most effort to abolish foreign pilotage in China, are being vigorously promoted by certain foreigners occupying key positions. It is said that the goal of their actions is to take a permanent solution, to ensure that the status of foreign pilots in China has a more effective basis under certain circumstances. The method of their actions is to inherit the mantle of Robert Hart, the Inspector General of Customs of the former Qing Dynasty. Because foreign pilots in Shanghai and other places originally had no basis in unequal treaties, it was only through Robert Hart's strategy of colluding internally and externally that he deceived the vague approval of the former Qing Dynasty Prime Minister's Office, and from then on, national rights and national defense were lightly lost, and the Chinese people who received its benefits have endured hardship for seventy years. Hart at the time used a small trick, claiming to China that he would transfer the power of selection and supervision of pilots to the River Affairs Department under his jurisdiction. But in reality, the River Affairs Department's supervision of the pilots was not responsible to China, but to the consuls of the treaty countries and the foreign general chambers of commerce. In fact, from beginning to end, training and selection were never given to the Chinese people. The Prime Minister's Office was lifeless and did not understand the conspiracy, and was played by Hart in the palm of his hand. This page of history of losing sovereignty and humiliating the country is something to sigh over. Now it is heard that the plan of these people is to preserve Robert Hart's legacy, and their steps are divided into two types. The first step is to use the good name of the Customs Service as a Chinese national official to anesthetize all parties with what Hart used to fool the former Qing Dynasty Prime Minister's Office, so that the Customs Service or its subordinate River Affairs Department can still hold the power of pilot supervision and selection. On the one hand, the wording of the treaty country's consuls is deliberately removed to avoid opposition from the Chinese people. At the same time, the foreign general chambers of commerce are also allowed to participate on the grounds that foreign ships employ the most pilots, and the Chinese general chambers of commerce are used as a foil. Directly and indirectly, they want to achieve the purpose of foreigners monopolizing the selection of pilots in our country. The second step is to use the excuse that our country temporarily lacks the necessary pilot talent, to ensure that nationals of all treaty countries with ships entering and leaving can apply to the pilotage bureau in Chinese ports to become pilots, and beautifully call it the implementation of equal treatment between China and foreign countries. Although the fox and rabbit are cunning, the dagger will eventually be revealed. The association has silently observed the foreigners' plan. No matter how sweet and pleasing their words are, no matter how strong and sufficient their reasons are, the reality is that they are stealing our country's rights. The position of pilot is of great importance to national rights and national defense, and of minor importance to the people's livelihood. How can it be easily sacrificed for a few pleasing terms or sophistical theories? Fortunately, the association is not living in a drunken dream. At this critical moment for the life and death of the country and individuals, it will definitely oppose to the death. The first step of this plan is to achieve its second step, that is, to achieve the permanent occupation of pilotage rights in all ports of our country by foreigners. The facts are obvious and can be seen clearly. Otherwise, the so-called Customs Service should be responsible for organizing taxation, and the River Affairs Department should only be limited to managing port affairs. As for selecting pilots, what does it have to do with them? However, Mr. Hart did not spare his efforts to take on this burden, and our country's rights were unknowingly lost for seventy years. Is this not a loyal minister and good friend of our country and our people, and one that we should always remember? Now that there are many who want to be the second Robert Hart, if we are not insane, who can fail to be wary of the lessons of the past? I think that our government is dedicated to washing away the shame of the Qing Dynasty's loss of sovereignty and humiliation, and will certainly not be moved by the floating words of good people, and fall into the enemy's plan to permanently occupy our country's pilotage rights. Moreover, all foreign customs officers and river affairs officers themselves are encroaching on our country's rights, and have been borrowing for a long time without returning, turning guests into hosts. The old man of Chu is sad, and Qiu Ming is single-minded. Is there any more tragic thing in the world than this? However, the reason for their existence is based on unequal treaties, which are originally examples of abolition and overthrow. In the past, there was the late Premier's will, and recently there have been the National Congress and the government's declaration, all of which take the abolition of unequal treaties as the most important task for the government and the people in the future. Should the foreign customs officers and river affairs officers under the protection of this kind of unequal treaty, and the pilot selection system monopolized by the customs officers and river affairs officers, be abolished immediately? Anyone with common sense will certainly have no doubt. Unless they are consciously traitors, they will not dare to advocate sophistry after carefully reading the late Premier's will, and in the presence of the national public opinion meeting and supervision, in order to implement the traitorous and self-enriching plans of Li Wan-yong and his like. The association thinks that the officials in power are the fathers and brothers of the people and the pillars of the party and the country, and they must have a strategy to secure the country and seize foreign land, and to relieve the people of permanent suffering. If children are subjected to violence from the outside, they will return and appeal to their fathers and brothers. Now that foreign pilots have this conspiracy to permanently occupy our territory, which is a matter of life and death for Chinese sailors, especially since the position of pilot is related to national defense, which everyone knows, it is not comparable to ordinary occupations. Therefore, we must present the information we have obtained in full, in order to prepare the government's plan to prevent problems before they occur and to control the enemy invisibly. And please, in accordance with the spirit of abolishing unequal treaties recently resolved by the National Congress, promptly issue an order stipulating that pilots in all Chinese ports should be appointed by Chinese nationals, and to set the shortest possible period to recover all existing foreign occupied pilotage powers in various ports, so as to avoid foreign coveting, and national rights and national defense can be permanently secured. Whether what is said is appropriate, please give a clear instruction, so that we may comply.

Discussions on the National Products Market Case Have Yielded Results 95

Closing and Operations to be Resolved Separately

All Employees Organize Mobile Propaganda

The National Products Market, which was ordered to close by the Public Concession, has had satisfactory results after repeated discussions by the negotiating committee, the Chinese directors, the municipal advisor, and the chairman of the municipal chamber of commerce. The negotiating committee will send personnel to the municipal government again today to petition. All employees will organize a mobile propaganda team for national products and are preparing to depart within a few days. The situation yesterday is recorded separately below.

Discussion Results: The National Products Market Negotiating Committee, Ren Jinpin, Zhang Zilian, and others, have been discussing methods with the Chinese directors of the Public Concession, Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, the municipal advisor Wu Jingxiong, He Dequi, the chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Wang Xiaolai, and the committee members, Fang Jiaobo, etc. The results are said to be that the market's closure and the funds for future operations will be resolved in two parts. The issue of closure will be addressed once the Public Concession's report is sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which will then make a fair and appropriate statement. As for the future operations of the market, it must strengthen its organization. The leaders of the business community have all agreed to actively assist. After the closure issue is resolved, the market will surely have new developments to comfort social expectations.

To Petition Again: The National Products Market Negotiating Committee sent Dong Jusun to the Lawyers Association yesterday. The standing members of the association, Tan Yigong and Li Cishan, and the executive members, Yu Zhongluo and Zhao Zuwei, received him. The association will prepare a written report on the circumstances of the Public Concession's order to close, in order to provide legal assistance after a meeting to discuss it. Also, because the case has already been protested by the municipal government, Liu Musu and Chen Weixin will be sent to the municipal government today to petition, requesting a prompt solution.

Mobile Propaganda: All employees of the National Products Market have been holding joint meetings for days to discuss the aftermath and, for the sake of publicizing the Public Concession's unreasonable order to close and maintaining the employees' livelihoods, have organized a mobile propaganda team for national products, which is scheduled to depart within a few days. Its organization is as follows: (1) Name: National Products Market Mobile Propaganda Team for National Products. (2) Purpose: (A) To sell national products. (B) To vigorously publicize the circumstances of the imperialists' unreasonable order to close. (C) To report on the progress of negotiations. (3) Organization: Jointly organized by the employees and manufacturers of the China National Products United Market. (4) Location: The area along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, with the capital as the final destination. (5) Duration: Return to Shanghai five days before the victory of the negotiations and the definite date of reopening. (6) Expenses: Divided into travel expenses, food expenses, and miscellaneous expenses. No other expenses may be incurred. (7) Promotional materials: Provided by the negotiating committee. (8) Goods: Controlled by the business department. Manufacturers will control their own goods. (9) Work: All levels will cooperate fully. (10) Goods: Cosmetics, knitwear, toothbrushes, cotton textiles, medicines, cloth, towels, undershirts. (11) Selling price: Should be set at the lowest possible limit.

Keel Laying Ceremony Held for the Pinghai Warship Yesterday 96

Chen Shaokuan Personally Hammered the First Rivet

The Navy Continues to Build Uninterruptedly

The Navy's Pinghai warship held its keel laying ceremony yesterday morning (28th) at 8:00 a.m. Chen Shaokuan, the Navy Deputy and Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, led the captains of the Yixian, Ziqiang, Dingan, and Jiankang warships, Chen Hongtai, Qiu Shizhong, Fang Ying, as well as the supervisors and the commander of the guard battalion, Ye Baoqi, to the site. Mr. Chen personally hammered the first rivet, and the captains of the warships each hammered a rivet in turn. Then they took photos, and the ceremony was completed. The ship is 340 feet long and 39 feet wide, and is the largest ship under construction in recent years. The navy is constantly building, and each ship is larger than the last, which is an excellent phenomenon. However, although the keel of the ship has been laid, the finances are still very difficult, and there is no great certainty. Mr. Chen's painstaking efforts are truly commendable.

Commissioner Zhang to Depart for Europe This Morning to Inspect Financial Administration 97

Chen Qicai, the Director of the Budgeting Office of the National Government, has specially dispatched Mr. Zhang Jun (Zhifu) to Europe to investigate the financial administration of various European countries. Mr. Zhang is a Bachelor of Commerce from the University of Edinburgh in the United Kingdom. This time he was appointed as a commissioner to inspect financial administration. He was approved to take the Fengtian Maru this morning (29th) and transfer to Russia from Dalian. He will first go to Poland and Germany for inspection, and then go to the United Kingdom, France, Italy, and other countries. Mr. Zhang is quite familiar with financial experts and government officials in Europe, and the results of this trip will surely be satisfactory.

Meeting on Dredging the Yu Canal 99

Regarding the Yu Canal in Shanghai County, the County Government previously ordered that dredging be temporarily postponed for one year. The Yu Canal Dredging Works Committee believes that this year will begin soon and preparations should be made in a timely manner to facilitate progress. Therefore, at 10:00 a.m. yesterday, the third meeting of the Canal Works Committee was held at the Third District Office of Beiqiao. Gong Quanxing, a representative of the County Construction Bureau, and Yang Fulin, Peng Zhaotang, and 19 others attended, chaired by Yang Fulin, to discuss and resolve various proposals. (1) The County Government submitted a proposal to straighten the bend. Whether it can be done. The meeting decided to do so, and Sun Ruisun, Yang Shunfan, Wang Benda, Peng Weiren, and Chen Bingxun were elected to work with Section Chief Gong of the Construction Bureau to gather at the Second District Office at 9:00 a.m. on the 30th of this month to conduct an on-site survey, assess the compensation for losses due to the straightening, and report to the meeting for submission to the County for handling. (2) The County Government submitted a proposal on how to handle the objections raised by the people of the First, Third, Yang, and Erxiang villages regarding the dredging of the Yu Canal, citing precedents. The meeting decided that the matter concerned a settled case and was difficult to change. The meeting should submit a report to the County Magistrate instructing the First District Office to provide thorough guidance. (3) The Third District Office submitted a proposal from citizens Zou Zongmeng and others of the Twentieth Ward, requesting that the ward not benefit from the Yu Canal's irrigation and that it be changed to a grant. The meeting decided to handle it according to the previous case and hand it over to the Third District Office for handling. (4) Dredging progress chart and schedule. The meeting decided to set the following dates: (1) Period for surveying and registering each ward: July 1 to August 15. (2) Allocation of the amount of earthwork to be excavated in each ward: August 16 to September 15. (3) Date for preparing to start work: September 16 to September 25. (4) Transport of materials for dam construction, driving in the Zhongshan stake and side stake, plotting the map, and bailing out water: September 26 to October 25. (5) Excavation of all earthwork: October 26 to December 25. (6) Inspection: January 1, 21st year. (7) Removal of waterwheels and dam materials: January 2 to January 11, 21st year. (8) Handling of concluding matters: January 12 to January 31, 21st year. The meeting requested the County Government to issue a circular to the Construction Bureau and the First, Second, Third, and Sixth District Offices to complete the work on time. (5) Fisherman representative Shi Musheng and others voluntarily subsidized the canal dredging expenses and requested approval for a fishing monopoly. The meeting decided that there was no precedent to follow and it was difficult to approve.

Pan Gongzhan and Tang Demin to Propose Two Important Cases at the Municipal Assembly 100

The Municipal Assembly of the entire city has been scheduled to open on July 1st. Delegates Pan Gongzhan and Tang Demin from the three districts, deeply aware of the significant impact of cultural expertise and social education on the nation's destiny, will propose two important cases for discussion and adoption by the assembly. The first case is a request to the central government to order the Ministry of Education to establish a Central Printing Bureau to compile various textbooks for schools at all levels nationwide, to develop cultural undertakings and unify national thought. The document is as follows: (A) Rationale: Education is the foundation of a nation, and the printing bureau is the vehicle of culture. To seek the strength and prosperity of the country, education must be popularized and the intelligence of the people enhanced. To seek the stability of social order, national consciousness must tend toward unity. The trend of national consciousness is closely related to the supply of various book materials. Therefore, running a bookstore, though a small matter, carries heavy responsibilities. Since the establishment of the school system in our country, the need for new books was mostly reliant on the Commercial Press, Chung Hwa Book Company, and other bookstores. In the last decade or so, spurred by world trends and changes in the political situation, bookstores have sprung up everywhere like mushrooms after rain. This phenomenon is indeed a clear testament to the progress of China's cultural undertakings. However, many of these bookstores are oblivious to the active significance of the book industry for national culture, prioritizing profit. Due to mutual competition, they either innovate to seek sales or create differences to appear superior. They lack a consistent and pure proposition and a national and ethnic perspective. School teachers either favor strange and deceitful rhetoric, innovating and showing off, or are stuck in the old ways, complacent and self-enclosed. In the same era, those who bear the important task of enlightening future generations have vastly different ideas, separated by several generations, which is hardly surprising. According to a survey and statistics from the Municipal Education Bureau, in the subject of Chinese language alone, about one hundred and several dozen types of textbooks are used in secondary schools nationwide. Although there are many good books among them, most have been formally reviewed and issued by the government. However, the compilers and authors are not uniform in their personnel or objectives, and young students learn differently, leading to different trends. Therefore, today, the social psyche and the thinking of young people in our country can be described as tangled threads, extremely complex. The impact of this extends to political disputes, social unrest, and the decline of national morality, all of which are deeply related. Our party, adhering to the teachings of the late Premier, bears the important mission of realizing the Three People's Principles. If we do not seek unity in national thought, then political unity will become a hollow and dangerous situation. Now, to enhance the people's understanding of the Three People's Principles and to seek effectiveness in school education, for the sake of unifying national thought and revitalizing national spirit, at this time of complex minds and divergent theories, it is urgent to find ways to remedy the situation. The most efficient and practical way to remedy this is to gather various specialized talents with rich knowledge and experience, and to establish a Central Printing Bureau to compile various textbooks for schools at all levels nationwide, using the theory of the Three People's Principles and the newly established education policies of the central government as the standard for compilation. This will allow the thoughts of young students across the country to be cultivated unconsciously, fostering a life consciousness of national struggle, sacrifice, and creation, and achieving the effect of one virtue and one custom. Then, the prosperity of the country and the nation can be expected soon. (B) Methods: (1) First, the Editorial and Review Department of the Ministry of Education should be expanded into two departments: Editorial and Review. Teachers of various subjects with rich knowledge and experience from universities and primary and secondary schools nationwide should be selected (selection methods will be determined separately) with preferential treatment. They will be given a deadline to compile textbooks and reference books for each subject according to the curriculum standards set by the ministry (the existing curriculum standards are mostly impractical and should be revised separately). Scholars with accumulated learning scattered throughout the country, known for their writings, should also be recruited and given preferential positions to reward them. (2) Next, the Central Printing Bureau should be established. All books compiled and approved by the Ministry of Education will be printed and distributed by the bureau. (3) After the printing and distribution of various textbooks, the Ministry of Education should immediately issue an order requiring all schools nationwide to adopt them uniformly and absolutely not purchase other books. (4) In addition to establishing a headquarters in Shanghai or the capital, the Central Printing Bureau should also establish branch offices in each province. (5) The Central Printing Bureau will be directly under the jurisdiction and command of the Ministry of Education. Branch offices in each province, in addition to being under the control of the headquarters, must also be under the direct command of the education department of each province. (6) The books compiled and printed by the Central Printing Bureau should be as inexpensive as possible to reduce the burden on poor students. (7) The amount of full funding and detailed methods can be planned separately. (To be continued)

Railway Bureau Warns Employees to Be Commercialized 101

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration posted a notice yesterday at various stations, stating that the railway business is essentially commercial in nature. Although the administration belongs to the country, its operations should be equivalent to those of a business. Employees should adopt a commercial spirit when dealing with merchants and the public to avoid mutual alienation. This railway is located in a vital area of the Southeast, and internal and external employees should interact with merchants and the public with sincerity, so that the interests of both parties can be mutually advanced. The Bureau, in compliance with the Ministry's orders to rectify railway operations, has repeatedly instructed employees to strictly comply. Now that the railway business is becoming increasingly busy, internal and external employees may still disregard official orders and mistreat merchants and the public. In addition to issuing a strict notice again, a public announcement is hereby made: if any railway employee neglects their duties or acts improperly, anyone may report the facts. Once verified, they will be punished without leniency. However, the employees are busy with their duties and may inevitably have times when they are not able to attend to every detail. Merchants and the public should also be understanding. If someone uses this as an excuse to be picky or deliberately make things difficult, the Bureau will not be able to manage everything. This is hereby announced.

Page 14

the Yangtze River, resulting in a reduction of vessels on the Yangtze River route. Commissioner Guo Waifeng had gone to Beijing to request their return. Ministry of Railways Yesterday Ordered Two Railway Administrations 103

To Rectify Railway Affairs and Restrict the Hiring of Personnel

The Ministry of Railways issued an order yesterday to the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations, stating: "For the purpose of issuing orders and implementing them, rectifying railway affairs begins with the hiring of personnel. While there is no shortage of skilled and experienced staff in the various railway departments, there are also many who advance through connections and achieve nothing. If restrictions are not strictly enforced and thorough reviews are not conducted, how can railway affairs be brought to a prosperous state? Now, three standards for entry are specified for compliance: (1) The railway is a specialized undertaking. In the future, mid-level and above, as well as key lower-level staff, should not be appointed unless they have sufficient knowledge and qualifications to prevent opportunistic advancement. (2) Employees who have served for many years and have not been derelict in their duties should not be replaced lightly to retain experienced personnel. When filling vacancies or reducing staff, the merits and demerits of performance and the seniority of qualifications should be weighed as the basis for promotion or demotion. (3) The appointment and dismissal of staff should be carried out in accordance with the general rules of organization and all other established regulations without encroachment to maintain discipline. The above articles should be strictly followed. In the future, if there is favoritism or abuse in guaranteeing positions, or if personnel are employed in violation of their talents, or if there are solicitations or personal requests in hiring, once discovered, strict disciplinary action will be taken. The chairman and director of the committee should especially set an example and refrain from abusing their authority, lest they cause public criticism. This is greatly hoped. This order."

Zou Bingwen Talks About the Recent Situation of the Commodity Inspection Bureau 108

Will Send Personnel to Japan to Inspect Raw Silk

Tea Inspection to Be Implemented Next Month

The Daily News reported that the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry has been established for two years and has spared no effort in conducting commodity inspections. Yesterday, a reporter from the Daily News interviewed Director Zou Bingwen to inquire about the latest situation, which is recorded as follows:

Inspecting Raw Silk: Japanese commodity inspections do not differentiate between grades of raw silk. However, starting from January 1st next year, they will be divided into several grades, including superior and secondary. The Bureau also plans to emulate this method for raw silk inspections. It will send technical officials to Japan to inspect the country's raw silk inspection situation to learn from their experience and improve its own methods.

Improving Sugar Inspection: The sugar inspection conducted by the Bureau starting on the 15th of this month has yielded good results. When grain merchants transport sugar to the docks, they must report to the Bureau, which will send personnel to inspect it. However, handling various procedures with customs during sugar inspection is quite troublesome and inconvenient. The Bureau recently discussed changing the procedures with customs to make them more convenient. The discussion is currently underway, and a satisfactory result should be obtained soon.

Tea Inspection: The Bureau is also preparing for tea export inspection, which is expected to be implemented in the middle of next month. According to Director Zou, who spoke to the reporter from the Daily News, China's tea exports have not improved in recent years. This is related to the competition from foreign merchants, and the lack of improvement in domestic tea planting and manufacturing methods is also a major reason. Furthermore, there are often profit-seeking merchants who sell inferior goods as superior ones, causing a loss of international trade credit, which has led to a decline in business. The purpose of this tea inspection is to remove the dross and preserve the essence, and to restore China's former status.

Anhui Official Arrested in Shanghai 111

Lai'an County Magistrate Wang Shao-yi

Embezzled More Than 9,000 Yuan of Public Funds

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, Chen, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, received a secret telegram from the Anhui Provincial Department of Finance stating that Wang Shao-yi, the magistrate of Lai'an County, had embezzled more than 9,800 yuan of public funds and absconded to Shanghai, hiding in Room 78 of the Dadong Hotel in the Yong'an Company on Nanjing Road in the Public Concession. He was requested to secretly dispatch officers, together with the police, to arrest Wang and then escort him back to the case for interrogation. After receiving the telegram, Director Chen immediately handed it to Lu Ying, the captain of the detective team, for proper handling. Subsequently, in the afternoon, squad leader Qi Haitian of the detective team, along with detectives Han Jingxiang and Lu Ruicheng, first secretly investigated the Dadong Hotel. However, there was no one named Wang in Room 78. They checked directly to Room 84, where Wang Shao-yi was indeed registered. Squad leader Qi immediately contacted the old Zha Gate police and Western detectives to arrest Wang and temporarily detain him at the police station. After a brief interrogation by the police chief, Wang confessed that he was 40 years old and from Guizhou. Squad leader Qi reported back to the captain and then to the director, who approved the preparation of documents for extradition today, pending the arrival of documents from the Anhui Provincial Department of Finance for disposal.

Survey of Autumn Agricultural Production in the Urban Area 112

Total Value of Over 3.97 Million Yuan

The Municipal Social Bureau, considering that countries around the world have meticulous statistics and detailed reports on the annual harvest of agricultural production for the public to explore, formulated a harvest survey form for major autumn crops last year for a practical survey. The statistics have now been completed. It is reported that last year's total cotton production in the city was 162,304 dan, valued at approximately 2,214,621 yuan. The rice harvest was 331,221 dan, valued at approximately 1,531,570 yuan. The bean harvest was 42,072 dan, valued at approximately 222,091 yuan. The total value was 3,978,282 yuan. However, the Yinxiang and Yangjing districts are not included, as these two districts are adjacent to the city and have less agricultural land. Therefore, they are omitted. It is further clarified that the entire areas of South Shanghai and Zhabei are market areas.

For the National Products Market Case

If citizens believe that the measures taken by the Public Works Department on sanitation, fire control, and construction are inappropriate or unacceptable, the Shanghai Municipal Government should review and arbitrate. 6. (2) Regarding the illegal closure of the national products market by the Public Works Department, it was resolved to notify all citizens of the city to unite and support the government as a backup for negotiations. (3) Regarding the current dispute over the national products market, which is due to the poor organization of the Public Works Department, it was resolved to send a letter to the Chinese directors stating that Chinese people should participate in the organizational committees to improve everything in the engineering, sanitation, and fire departments. (4) Before the national products market can be resolved, the following measures were decided: A. Convene a citizens' representative assembly on a regular basis. B. Notify each district branch to send three to five representatives to participate. C. Proposals for the citizens' representative assembly include: 1. Boycott British goods. 2. International publicity. 3. Suspend all donations until a satisfactory resolution is reached. (5) Regarding the progress of the association's affairs, it was decided that the association's meetings will be held every Thursday, and the time will be changed to 1:00 PM, with lunch provided. (5) Regarding whether to participate in Yu Qiaqing's 50th anniversary of living in Shanghai, it was decided that participation is appropriate. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Zhenhai County Magistrate Cao Suspended After Accusation 118

Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association Telegraphs Province to Vindicate Him

Zhenhai County Magistrate Cao Boquan was recently impeached by Shao Hongji, a supervisory committee member of the Supervisory Yuan, based on an accusation by Ding Qinghua and others, representatives of the villagers of Lingyan Village in Zhenhai, alleging that local bullies extorted money, judges neglected their duties, and the county magistrate was negligent. The National Government telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government, ordering the suspension of County Magistrate Cao Boquan, the trial judge Hu Jiajun, and the village chief Li Jinglian, pending investigation and punishment. The Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai, based on a telegram from Lou Qiliang and other gentry and merchants in Zhenhai requesting vindication, sent a telegram to the Zhejiang Provincial Government yesterday.

The telegram reads: "To Chairman Zhang and all members of the Zhejiang Provincial Government: We have received a joint telegram from Lou Qiliang, Chen Tingjun, Liu Xinyin, and others from Zhenhai, stating that they were shocked to read in the newspaper that County Magistrate Cao Boquan had been ordered to suspend his duties. They found County Magistrate Cao to be honest, fair, diligent, and possessing a revolutionary spirit that is widely praised. This sudden suspension, due to being implicated in a case involving the former trial judge Hu, not only subjects County Magistrate Cao to an unjust grievance but also brings misfortune to our county's politics. Therefore, we jointly telegraph, requesting your esteemed council to uphold justice, vindicate County Magistrate Cao's grievance, and protect this virtuous magistrate for the people of our county. The telegram further states that the gentlemen named are all fair and upright gentry, sufficient to represent the majority of public opinion. Based on the above, we urgently telegraph your government for consideration, earnestly requesting your kind understanding and prior reinstatement to appease public opinion.

Respectfully, Yu Hede, Chairman of the Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai, and all committee members.

Fire at Nan Yu Tai 119

Nan Yu Tai Sugar and Food Store, located at No. 173 inside the Guoma Road, 16 Pu, Nanshi, has been established for many years. The store is a two-story, double-entry building. Besides being used as a storefront and warehouse, the northern part of the upper floor is where the store owner's family resides. Yesterday at around 4:00 AM, a fire suddenly broke out in the rear storage room, filled with grass goods. In an instant, smoke filled the air, and the fire broke through the roof. When the Firefighting Joint Association heard about it, it rang the alarm. Soon, firefighting associations from various districts dispatched pump trucks to the scene to draw water and extinguish the fire. It took about an hour for the fire to be extinguished.

During this incident, all four buildings of the store were completely destroyed by the fire. Fortunately, the store's staff and warehouse staff noticed the fire early and rushed to escape. Among them, one group jumped down from the veranda. In the chaos, they were careless and fell from a height, injuring their legs. The owner and his family were startled from their dreams and found that the staircase had already been burned. They climbed onto the roof of the neighboring house via a clothes-drying rack and were able to escape. Afterwards, Liu Xuezhou, a guard from the 10th Post of the area, took Xu Dafu, a Ningbo native working at the store, back to the First District Headquarters of the camp. During the preliminary interrogation, Xu stated that he did not know the cause of the fire. However, the loss to the store was estimated to be over 10,000 taels of silver. As the incident concerned a fire, it was ordered that an official document be prepared and submitted to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Shanghai Residents Passionate About Swimming, Swimming Pools Crowded 120

Over Four Thousand Attendees Yesterday

Water Change Tomorrow, Closed for One Day

The Hongkou open-air swimming pool is established by the Public Works Department. The pool area is 100 yards long and 30 yards wide, accommodating over a thousand people. It opened last month. Anyone, regardless of age, without contagious diseases, can enter and swim for two dimes. Shanghai residents, lacking swimming venues, flock there daily during this hot weather, often reaching over a thousand people. Yesterday was Sunday, and the weather was very hot, so the number of attendees reached over four thousand. The pool's manager, seeing that the pool could not accommodate everyone, posted a "Full" sign and locked the main gate, opening a side door for swimmers leaving. By 2:00 PM, it was closed, and within ten minutes, five to six hundred people were waiting outside the gate. There were three attempts to squeeze into the side door, almost leading to verbal altercations with the manager. Fortunately, most of the swimmers were athletes from commercial and academic circles, possessing high character, so nothing untoward happened. When the bell rang four times, the number of swimmers in the pool gradually decreased, and the main gate was opened to allow latecomers to enter. The pool water is tested daily by the Department of Health. If the water contains toxic substances or is turbid, it will be changed. Tomorrow is the day for water change, so swimming enthusiasts need not make the trip.

The Sensational Murder Case in Western Shanghai Solved 121

Old Widow Has Two Lovers

Zhao Qilang Kills Rival in Jealousy

Kong Chengrong Died Terribly

Widow Claims to Be Pregnant

On the morning of the 15th of this month, an unidentified male corpse, assassinated and suffering four knife wounds, with his genitals cut off, was discovered in a deserted area near the Lime Kiln north of Xiaoshadu Creek in Western Shanghai (details already reported in this newspaper). After the incident occurred, society took notice, and it created a sensation for a time. Later, the deceased's brother, Kong A'er, applied to the District Court, identifying the deceased as his younger brother, Kong Chengrong. He was granted permission to collect the coffin and bury the body. Now, District Chief Ren of the Sixth District has strictly ordered all detectives to tighten their efforts to arrest the perpetrators. The murderer, the adulterous woman, and those involved have all been apprehended, and the truth has come to light, confirming that the incident was caused by a love triangle, leading to such a tragic and bizarre event. The details are recorded below.

District Chief Ren Strictly Orders Arrest of Perpetrators

After the incident occurred, it created a sensation in society. District Chief Ren believed that the murderer's cruel methods were truly detrimental to social morality. Based on the initial investigation, the trail of blood led from behind the Fuxin Third Factory all the way to the Lime Kiln. Although it could be determined that the murder site was behind the factory (which is within the Fourth District's jurisdiction), the discovery site was within his jurisdiction. Therefore, he strictly ordered all detectives to tighten their efforts to arrest the perpetrators and severely punish them as a warning to the unruly.

Insight Obtained, Truth Revealed

Liu Shaoqing, the head of the district's detective team, and detectives Cao Chuqiao, Gan Xixin, Tang Bingxiang, Sun Rongxuan, and Hu Rui, after receiving orders, began investigating. Later, thanks to Cao Chuqiao's tireless research, they received a report from an informant, claiming that the case involved Zhao Du Shi, a widow living at No. 3, Nian'an Lane, Sheng'an Li, Maojia Lane, Nanshi. She was initially in love with Zhao Qilang. However, recently, the woman abandoned her old love and became acquainted with the deceased, Kong Chengrong. Therefore, Zhao held hatred in his heart and killed Kong. The informant also stated that Zhao was hiding at the Yuqing shop in the Haichao Temple. Only then did Detective Cao learn the details. Suddenly, they heard that the police station of the First District had already arrested Zhao Cailang, who is Zhao Qilang's brother. The detective team then requested the Third Branch of the First District to dispatch police officers to accompany them to the upstairs of the Yuqing tobacco and paper shop on the afternoon of the previous day. They apprehended Zhao Qilang on the spot and took him back to the Sixth District headquarters for temporary detention. Yesterday morning, the original team of detectives went to No. 143, Sanpailou Road, in the city and apprehended the adulterous woman, Zhao Du Shi, and her son, Zhao Jinrong, as well. They then went to Sheng'an Li and brought back Zhu Lao'er and Zhu Ye Shi, who lived with the woman, for questioning.

Old Widow Reveals the Truth

After separate interrogations by District Chief Ren, the widow stated that her surname was Wang, named Ye Shi (real surname Zhao Du Shi), 40 years old, from Changzhou. She currently resides at No. 23, Sheng'an Li, Maojia Lane. Her husband passed away two years ago. She is a second wife. Her husband had a son named Jinrong from his previous wife, who had not borne any children. She has a cohabitant, Zhu Lao'er, from Haimen. In the first month of the lunar calendar, Zhao Qilang, a fellow villager, suddenly started visiting her home. From then on, they became acquainted, and before long, she was seduced into an affair. On the night of the 20th of the first month, she had intercourse with Zhao once. Afterwards, he stayed at her place several times. On the afternoon of the 16th of the second month, Zhao borrowed ten yuan from her, falsely claiming that he wanted to make a robe. On the afternoon of the 16th of the third month, Zhao came to her house again and forced her to have intercourse. Because it was a Sunday, her son had to return home, and it was in broad daylight, she refused and went to the living room. He then lay alone on her bed. Shortly after, her son returned home, entered the room, and saw someone on her bed. He became furious and asked who it was. She replied that she didn't know. Her son then drove him out, and Zhao also claimed that he would never come again, which led to his release. Later, she fell in love with Kong Chengrong (the deceased, and Zhao were also acquainted), who lived with her, and had intercourse with Kong on the 16th of the fourth month. On the night of the 27th of the fourth month, Kong was talking at her house when Zhao Qilang barged in. She locked the door and sternly rejected him. On the afternoon of the 29th, she went to Kong Chengrong's house in Xiaonanmen and saw Kong and Zhao leaving together. She then returned home. Later, not seeing Kong, she found Zhao on the 2nd of the fifth month and asked where Kong was. At first, he said he didn't know, then he claimed he was sick in the hospital. She repeatedly questioned him, and Zhao suddenly became angry and said that if she asked again, he would kill her too! (This statement is ironclad proof that he is the murderer). Hearing this, she realized the danger and had to return home. Later, she heard about the case in the newspaper, so she became very anxious and hid at A Gen's house on Sanpailou Road. Her son, Zhao Jinrong, 29 years old, originally from Pudong, works in printing. His father is deceased. Du Shi is his stepmother. He returns home once a week. On Sunday, the 23rd of the fourth month, he returned home and saw Zhao Qilang lying on his mother's bed. He slapped him once. Later, because he swore never to come again, he let him go. Later, he learned that his mother had an affair with Kong Chengrong. He was about to investigate when he read in the newspaper that Kong had been killed. He knew that Zhao must have been jealous and resorted to this tactic. He then wrote a letter to the Third Branch of the First District, stating that the Xiaoshadu murder case was committed by Zhao Qilang, signed with the pseudonym Leng. The murderer, Zhao Qilang, 36 years old, from Haimen, who lives at the Yuqing shop in the Haichao Temple and works as a cook, denied the murder and evaded the question. Zhu Lao'er and his wife, Ye Shi, gave testimonies consistent with the adulterous woman's statements, proving that Kong must have been killed by Zhao. After obtaining these testimonies, District Chief Ren believed that the case was clear, and the murderer could not deny it. He decided to prepare a document and hand him over to the Public Security Bureau today for interrogation.

What to Do with the Baby in Her Belly

The deceased, Kong Chengrong, was 36 years old, from Haimen, and originally lived upstairs in a tobacco and paper shop on Miezhu Street in Xiaonanmen. He had recently lost his wife. The day he was killed was the seventh week after his wife's death. Although he had only had an affair with the woman for a month, the woman was already pregnant. Yesterday, she shed tears in the headquarters, constantly asking what to do with the baby in her belly, expressing deep sorrow for Kong's death. Her son was crestfallen and seemed very ashamed.

Shanghai Has Been Extremely Hot for Days 122

The weather in Shanghai has been extremely hot for the past few days, with the temperature on the Fahrenheit thermometer rising to around 96 degrees. Yesterday was especially bad. From the morning, there was no breeze, making it exceptionally stuffy. Hawkers carrying goods and rickshaw pullers on the roads complained incessantly. However, those selling steam water, ice cream, and other cold items saw their profits triple. Watermelons were also available for sale (Guangdong goods), selling for 17 yuan per load. In the evenings, people cooling off on the roads were everywhere. Poor people, unable to sleep comfortably indoors due to the stifling heat, slept outdoors on balconies, at doorways, or on sidewalks.

Hua Zhen Company Sues Postal Bureau 123

Jadeite Parcel Lost by Postal Bureau

Demands Compensation of 2,400 Yuan

In the winter of 1927, Hua Zhen Company entrusted a jadeite parcel worth 2,400 yuan to the General Post Office for registration and sent it to New York, USA. However, it was delayed by postal officials and not sent, causing the recipient to wait for a long time without news. They telegraphed Hua Zhen for inquiries. When Hua Zhen investigated with the post office, the parcel could not be found. They demanded compensation at the price of the goods, but the post office refused. After repeated negotiations, the bureau only agreed to compensate ten francs based on Article 332 of the postal regulations. Hua Zhen felt that this was too much of a loss and refused to accept it. The post office then instructed them to wait for a report to the Ministry of Communications for review. More than three years have passed since then. Hua Zhen does not know whether it was reported to the ministry and can no longer wait. Therefore, they hired lawyer Qian Baohe to sue the Special District Court, requesting the Postal Bureau to compensate for the goods worth 2,400 yuan and the customs duties and postal taxes of 325 yuan paid for the parcel. Yesterday, Judge Yang of the Special Court summoned them for questioning. The post office hired lawyers Wang Zijian and Li Zuyu to defend and presented the postal regulations of China and the United States to counter the plaintiff's demands. Judge Yang believed that the case still needed investigation and adjourned it for further questioning.

Tian Shulan Lectures at the Border Development Association 124

Why Travel Around the Country?

The China Border Development Preparation Committee invited the national traveler Tian Shulan to lecture at No. 206, Wenyuan Fang, Aiyu Xian Road, Jinshenfu Road, at 11:00 AM yesterday on the topic of "Why I Want to Travel Around the Country." The association's chairman, Wang Yang, first reported on the organization's situation, followed by Tian's speech. He stated that he had aspired to travel the world since childhood. Whenever teachers spoke about the rich resources of Northeast China and Mongolia, he would discuss solutions with two or three classmates. Time flies, and now he can finally fulfill his long-cherished wish. The purpose of this trip around the country is sixfold: (1) To broaden his horizons by not fearing difficulties and venturing into barren lands. (2) To record facts and clarify the truth to provide reference for the world. (3) To harmonize ethnic groups to achieve the ideal of a great united world. (4) To practice enduring hardship and struggle. If the environment allows, further exploration should be undertaken. (5) This trip around the country is expected to last six years. If successful, he will return to Shanghai and plan a more ambitious trip around the world, which will take twice as long. If he has the ability, he will organize an expedition team to explore the North and South Poles and the peaks of the Himalayas. (6) The study of worldly affairs is endless. Today's new knowledge is tomorrow's historical data. He is determined to pursue his goals with unwavering perseverance and will not stop until he has thoroughly examined the geography and human conditions. This departure is either success or sacrifice. Tian's words were passionate and inspiring, moving the audience. Finally, guests Zhou Xiuquan and Zhao Shouyu offered words of encouragement, which were mostly pertinent. The event ended at 1:00 PM. It is said that Tian plans to depart from Shanghai at noon on July 1st.

Flour Boat Sinks in Storm 125

Two Boatmen Drown

Four Passengers Abducted

The flour boat Liu Baokui loaded 800 bags of flour in Shanghai and sailed to outside Wusongkou to unload cargo onto a foreign ship. In the afternoon of the previous day, at low tide, they started to sail. However, because the cargo carried by the ship had not been completely unloaded, Liu's boat was anchored beside the ship waiting to unload. Suddenly, yesterday morning, as dawn approached, a strong storm struck. For safety, Liu sailed to the shore to anchor and avoid the danger. At noon, Liu saw that the ship's cargo had been unloaded and immediately sailed closer to unload the cargo. While turning the boat, a strong gust of wind caused the entire boat to capsize. Liu and four boatmen fell into the water together. Fortunately, a small tugboat carrying passengers arrived and tried its best to rescue them. However, due to the strong wind and waves, rescue was difficult. Only three boatmen were rescued. Liu and another boatman were swept eastward and could not be rescued, presumably drowning. The entire cargo of flour sank to the bottom of the sea. Only the hull of the boat remained, drifting on the surface of the water. The boatmen hired a boat to search for Liu and the other boatman's bodies and reported to the cargo owner. By noon yesterday, a boat found Liu's body in Gaoqiao. The other boatman's body has not been found yet. The Life Saving Bureau has been notified to dispatch patrol boats to search for it.

Police Ban Swimming 126

Due to the hot weather in Shanghai in recent days, the waterfronts of the Huangpu River in Nanshi and the Suzhou Creek in northern Shanghai are often seen with children and adults swimming naked from the shore or floating bridges, chasing and splashing each other, in a state of great joy, as the sun sets. The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team believes that such swimming is not only unhygienic but also dangerous for their personal lives. Therefore, Chief Xu of the team has ordered all subordinate teams to inform their officers to strictly prohibit it.

Rice Boat Robbed at Lao Hong Port 127

Boat Owner and Son Swim to Safety

Four Passengers Abducted

Rice boat owner Zhu Xinmao loaded over a hundred stones of white rice in Changshu, intending to transport it to Waisha, Chongming, for sale. He also carried four passengers. At around 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the previous day, while sailing past Lao Hong Port outside of Songkou, they temporarily docked by the port due to unfavorable winds and tides. Before long, four or five pirate ships suddenly sailed towards them. Seeing this, the rice boat tried to raise anchor and escape, but the pirate ships had already approached and surrounded them. The pirates swarmed onto the rice boat, first emptying it of the rice it was carrying. Then, failing to find any silver, they forcibly took Zhu Xinmao, his son, and the four passengers onto the pirate ships. Seeing this, Zhu Xinmao and his son were terrified and took advantage of the pirates' inattention to jump into the port and swim to shore. Although the pirates fired shots into the water, they fortunately did not hit them, and they escaped unharmed. The pirates were furious and destroyed the rice boat, abandoning it in the port. They abducted the four passengers and fled. The rice boat has now floated to Qiyaokou. Yesterday, the local water police found and seized it. However, there is still no news of the abducted four passengers.

The Work-Study Center for Vagrants in Caohejing, Western Shanghai, was initiated by philanthropists such as Mr. Wang Yiting in Shanghai and opened in June of the 18th year of the Republic of China. To date, it has been two years, and there have been over six hundred vagrants and beggars sent from various places, almost reaching full capacity. The director of the center, Mr. Wu Zhinan, is thrifty, simple, deeply knowledgeable, and meticulous in his planning, putting in a great deal of effort. Yesterday afternoon, Ye Bingheng from the Wuzhou Gu Ben Soap Factory in Xujiahui, Chen Xiaomei from the Ninth District Party Department, Liu Yunfang, the director of the Second Branch of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Zhou Chengxiang, the captain of the Tenth Team of the South Shanghai District Guard, visited the center. Director Wu warmly welcomed them. The center is divided into three departments: document management and work, and nine sections: teaching, diagnosis, barbering, hygiene, security, inspection, visitation, discipline, and training. He then led them to inspect the east and west dormitories and the one, two, three, and four workshops. There are sewing, shoemaking, woodworking, straw work, metalworking, hat-making, box-pasting, and machine weaving sections. There is also a Jingxin Hall, where vagrants who are fierce and unruly and do not listen to instruction reside. Finally, there is a large lecture hall that can accommodate a thousand seats. Then, Director Wu rang the bell to gather all the vagrants and invited Mr. Ye and others to give speeches (the content of the speeches is omitted). The words were sincere and touching, moving the audience. Everyone left until six o'clock.

Yao Zhang Shi, the wife of the late actor Yao Junqing, and her daughter, Yao Shunxi, were previously sued by Li Xiuru, the female head of the Tianjin Modern Times, for allegedly luring Ren Shuzhen, her husband's concubine, and Chen Yindi, a fourteen-year-old girl, to sell themselves at the Xianrou Zhuang (a secret brothel) at No. 1, Linbi Fang, Changbin Road. Yao's wife and daughter then sued Li and Chen for fabricating facts and filing a false accusation. At that time, he already had one wife and two concubines, but he still hoped to take Shunxi as a concubine. Chen Yindi was also forced to move due to overdue rent. Unexpectedly, Li Xiuru invited Chen Yindi and hired lawyer Ye Feikang to file a lawsuit. Fortunately, the court was insightful and they were not陷害 harmed. However, the defendants publicly insulted them and should be held responsible. Please impose appropriate punishment according to Articles 180 and 325, Paragraph 1, of the Criminal Law. The case was heard by Judge Ge of the Special Court on the afternoon of the previous day. Both defendants avoided appearing in court. According to the plaintiffs' lawyer, Fan Qisheng, when Li Xiuru and others sued the plaintiffs in this case, they immediately filed a countersuit. Later, Li's suit was rejected by Judge Wu, and the court orally announced that a separate lawsuit would be filed regarding the countersuit. Therefore, the plaintiffs followed the court's instructions and filed this lawsuit. Judge Ge ruled that a countersuit had already been filed and had not been adjudicated. According to the Criminal Procedure Law, a case that has already been filed in the same court should not be heard. The circumstances of this case are consistent, and the court ruled that the case would not be accepted.

Car Brakes Failed

Girl's Parents Seek Compensation for Losses
