The incident was reported to Judge Zhu, who confirmed the facts of the case and ordered further investigation. The other day, the police summoned all parties involved to the French Concession Court for questioning. First, the head of the traffic department reported the background of the case. Then, Mr. D.V. Tappert, the lawyer representing the deceased's family, stated that the police investigation revealed that the defendant's car had faulty brakes, making it impossible to stop in time, leading to this tragic accident. In addition to requesting further investigation, regarding the private suit, the plaintiff stated that a total of over seven thousand yuan had been spent on his daughter from birth until now, and that the plaintiff couple had suffered immense emotional distress since their daughter's death. Therefore, they requested compensation of ten thousand yuan for their losses. The defendant, Guo Yuchun, testified that the girl had suddenly darted out from a side road, making it impossible for him to brake in time, causing the accident. His remaining testimony was evasive. The Chinese and Western judges ordered him to step down and await the judgment.

Conviction for Forced Prostitution 133

Wang Genbao and Wang Shenshi, pimps of the Zhiji brothel at No. 569 Ningbo Road, Weishui Lane, incited their adopted daughter, Xu Aidi, to remain in the brothel and forced her into prostitution after she divorced her husband, Yao Heshang. They also sought out Shen A'gen and his wife, Shen Yaoshi, acquaintances of theirs, to force their fifteen-year-old daughter, A'nan, into the flesh trade as well. The Lao Zha police station discovered the matter and detained the pimps and their sub-landlord, Qian Shouqing, handing them over to the Special District Court. The two girls were sent to the Jiliang Institute for care, pending sentencing. The other day, presiding Judge Zhou opened the court and sentenced Wang Genbao and Wang Shenshi to one year of imprisonment each, with a fine of two hundred yuan. If the fine could not be paid, it was to be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. Shen A'gen and Shen Yaoshi were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment, while Qian Shouqing was found not guilty.

Xu Ju Shun Bamboo Utensil Store Fire 138

Foreign Concession Cigars Must Be Registered and Supplemental Tax Paid 139

The Tobacco Exchange Guild Petitions for Remedial Measures

Yao Jiaqi, Director of the Shanghai Inspection Office of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Unified Tax Bureau, strictly inspected cigar and white cigarette sales in foreign concession tobacco shops. Many shops were found to be in violation, and letters were sent to the Tobacco Exchange Guild requesting assistance. The Guild's chairman, Chen Liangyu, Shen Weiting, and Dong Keliang, went to the Unified Tax Bureau to petition. The director agreed to negotiate and outlined the following remedial measures: (1) All existing plain cigars must be affixed with supplementary tax stamps to avoid penalties. (2) The number of stamps to be supplemented should be registered with the Guild, who would then obtain and affix the stamps. The stamps obtained cannot be of a lower grade than the tobacco they are affixed to. If any trickery is found, penalties will still be imposed. (3) The stamps will be obtained by the Guild and distributed to each shop for self-affixing. After affixing, they will be submitted to the Guild, where tax bureau officials will be dispatched to stamp them. (4) The tax grades are divided into six levels: (A) 1,000 cigars priced at 72 yuan 2 jiao or more are affixed with 45 yuan. (B) 1,000 cigars priced at 35 yuan 1 jiao or more are affixed with 22 yuan 5 jiao. (C) 1,000 cigars priced at 17 yuan 5 jiao 5 fen or more are affixed with 11 yuan 2 jiao 5 fen. (D) 1,000 cigars priced at 8 yuan 7 jiao 7 fen 5 li or more are affixed with 5 yuan 6 jiao 5 fen. (E) 1,000 cigars priced at 5 yuan 2 jiao 6 fen 5 li or more are affixed with 3 yuan. (F) 1,000 cigars priced at less than 5 yuan 2 jiao 6 fen 5 li are affixed with 2 yuan 2 jiao 5 fen. For quantities from 25 to 200 cigars, calculate proportionally.

Xishan Sojourners in Shanghai Pay Attention to Rebuilding the Guild Hall's Market Houses 140

The Jinting Guild Hall on Daxing Street, Xiaoximen, in this city, is a charitable organization of Xishan sojourners from Dongting in Shanghai. Outside the hall, there are over thirty old market houses and eight old bungalows, which have been in disrepair for years and are in danger of collapse. Therefore, the temporary executive committee of the guild hall decided to rebuild them and prepared a proposal and detailed architectural drawings. Luo Huanzhang, in his name, sent a letter to the custodians of the guild hall's land deed, the owners of Senji Yi, Jinyuan Mao, and Tongyuan Heng, requesting the land deed in order to mortgage it for funds to rebuild the market houses. Senji and others, due to the importance of the entrustment by the fellow villagers and the matter concerning the public, did not dare to hand over the deed without authorization and specially published a notice to solicit the opinions of the fellow villagers. An investigation revealed that the number of Xishan sojourners in Shanghai is close to two thousand, most of whom are in favor of the rebuilding, but oppose the proposal of the temporary executive committee. This is because after the implementation of the proposal, the rent collected in the future will only be enough to pay interest, and the principal will be repaid indefinitely. The guild hall's land will inevitably belong to those who advance the funds. Therefore, people are gathering to discuss a perfect plan. Half of the members of the temporary executive committee also expressed their sympathy. It is said that it has been decided to convene a meeting of all fellow villagers to discuss the matter.

Fire at Lange Third Lumber Mill 141

The British firm McBain & Co., located at No. 1 The Bund, established the Lange Lumber Mill seven years ago at No. 1489 Huade Road, east of Gaolang Bridge, using machinery to specially cut various applicable wood. Business was booming and large. As the materials produced could not meet the demand, a second factory was built next to the main factory, and a third factory was added opposite the main factory at the south end of Xiaobang. At 9:15 PM last night, a fire suddenly broke out in the sawing room of the third factory, quickly spreading and becoming unapproachable. Although fire brigades from Yangshupu and Central Xinzha rushed to put out the fire, everything on fire was wood, making it difficult to extinguish. It was not extinguished until 11:30 PM, lasting for more than two hours. Except for a small amount of material near the bank at the front, which was spared, the remaining machinery and wood were all burned to ashes. It is said that the loss has not yet been determined, but it is estimated to be over hundreds of thousands of yuan.

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Prohibits Private Publication of Seals by Labor Unions 142

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating that labor unions that have been approved for registration in accordance with the law have been issued a rectangular seal by the Bureau for identification. Recently, some labor unions that have not been approved for registration have privately copied the seal in an attempt to deceive. Therefore, it is hereby announced to all labor unions in the city, whether established or not, that from the date of this notice, labor unions that have not been approved for registration, but have been approved for establishment by the Municipal Party Department, are only allowed to use a long wooden stamp with the name of the union. Those that are still in the preparatory stage should also add the words "Preparatory Committee." Those that have already published rectangular seals must destroy them all and reprint them. If anyone dares to copy and use them privately, once verified, they will be prosecuted for counterfeiting seals. Do not say that you were not warned.

The First District of the County Seriously Handles Personal Registration 143

Wu Jingqing, the district chief of the first district of Shanghai County, is handling personal registration in this district very seriously. The following is a record of his notice to the people: Fellow citizens, personal registration is a major matter in the process of autonomy, and everyone should not ignore it. According to Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Personal Registration promulgated by the Ministry, the general categories of personal registration are divided into the following seven items: (1) birth, (2) death, (3) marriage, (4) inheritance, (5) separation, (6) migration, (7) disappearance. Fellow citizens, if any of the above events occur, you must apply for registration. The registration procedures are very simple. You only need to report to the nearest district office or township office/town office to apply for registration, free of charge. If you conceal and fail to report, you will be punished if found out.

Commercial News

Sharp Fluctuations in Last Week's Bullion Market 160

A Plunge of One Hundred and Ten Taels in a Single Week

Hit by the Declaration of Deferring War Debts

Major Players Dumped Stocks Uncontrollably; the Unprecedented and Severe Fluctuations in Last Week's Bullion Market Intensified into a Fierce Downturn, Seemingly Beyond Control.

This was Truly Caused by the Declaration of U.S. President Hoover's Proposal to Suspend War Debt Payments for One Year. It was Like a Bolt from the Blue, Triggering Terror in the Market, Stirring Up Panic, and Leaving People Helpless. Furthermore, Stock Prices on Various New York Exchanges Soared, and Overseas Silver Prices Skyrocketed. Large Bars Increased by More Than One Penny, and Silver Prices Jumped by More Than Two Cents. Consequently, Shanghai's Exchange Rates Also Rose Sharply, with the Pound Sterling Rate Increasing by One Penny and Seventy-Five Points, the U.S. Dollar Rate by Three and a Half Yuan, and the Japanese Yen Rate Plunging by Nineteen Points. The Actual Trading Prices of Banks All Loosened Excessively. The Shilling Rate Exceeded Four Pence. Gold Businesses Engaged in Hedging Aggressively Dumped Stocks, and Major Long Positions Were Eager to Sell Notes. Driven by the Environment, They Had to Endure the Pain and Liquidate Their Positions, Suffering Greatly. The Market Price Has Broken Through the 700 Tael Mark. From the Morning Opening of 792 Taels at the Beginning of the Week, to a Sudden Low of 690 Taels and 5 Mace at the Weekend, There Was a Difference of 101 Taels and 5 Mace. The Total Decline Was a Terrible 98 Taels and 6 Mace. Tracing Back to the Closing Price of 800 Taels and 0.006 Mace the Previous Weekend, It Was Calculated That in Just One Week, There Was a Sharp Drop of More Than 110 Taels, Which Was Truly Unimaginable. However, the Fluctuations During That Period Were Extremely Turbulent, With Swings of Ten to Twenty Taels Being Common. It Almost Felt Like Mountains Were Collapsing and Seas Were Sinking. It is Said That the Changes in Major Long and Short Positions Have Been Mutually Changing Recently. It Is Suspected That the Previous Swap Deals, as Well as the Speculation by Cantonese Banking Group Heng Xing and Others, Involved Taking Long Positions in July and Short Positions in August. All Those Who Had Not Completed the Swap Would Have to Settle the Public Orders According to the Regulations in Early July, That is, Receive Cash. Recently, Naked Positions Have Been Seen Rising, With Bullion Increasing by 15 Taels. The Largest Suppression of Bullion Settlement Prices Was More Than 90 Taels, the Smallest Was More Than 20 Taels, and Finally, It Was Around 50 Taels. The Future of the Gold Market is Feared to Still Have Violent Double Movements. The General Situation of the Week is Summarized Below.

Breaking the 700 Tael Mark Twice - On Monday (June 22), the Large Bar Silver Slightly Increased by 0.0625, the U.S. Silver Increased by 0.125, and the Shilling Gold Price Initially Dropped by 9 Taels and 1 Mace, to 791 Taels and 5 Mace. Next, It Was 92 Taels, Because the War Debt Was Postponed for One Year and U.S. Stocks Soared, People Were Terrified, With a Sense of Irreversible Decline. It Plummeted Terribly by 40 Taels, and at Noon, It Was Only 51 Taels and a Half. The Afternoon Was Even Weaker, Suddenly Becoming 730 Taels, Because the Indian Exchange Rate Rose Repeatedly. It Closed at 35 Taels, a Terrible Drop of 65 Taels and 6 Mace Compared to Last Friday (Saturday Was a Holiday for the Dragon Boat Festival, and There Was No Market). It Was Truly a Rare and Strange Change. There Was a Difference of 62 Taels Throughout the Day. Major Players Such as Wu, Lu, and Luo All Disposed of Their Holdings. The Next Day, the Large Bar Soared by 1.3125 Pence, and the Silver Price Increased by a Huge 2 Cents. The Initial Hanging Price of the Shilling Was Four Blocks Higher, and Then It Was Changed and Reduced Twice, Counting as One and a Half Blocks. The Internal Market Trend Diverged, Turning From Weak to Moderate, Showing a Slight Rebound, Which Was Unexpected. Fellow Traders Still Tried Their Best to Sell and Hedge Back Gold. As for the August Bullion, the Opening Price Was Slightly Down by 12 Taels, to 722 Taels. After That, the Buyers Seemed to Be Moving, and the Trend Rose, But There Were Ups and Downs. From Morning to Noon, There Were a Total of 29 Taels of Review. In the Afternoon, It Had Eased Out to 50 Taels, and the Closing Price Returned to 44 Taels, Returning 9 Taels More Than the Previous Day. It Was Truly a Trend of a Big Fall and a Small Rebound. On Wednesday, the Silver Market Shrank by 0.05625, the U.S. Silver by 0.0625, the Shilling Remained Unchanged, the Internal Market Seemed Loose, and Fellow Traders Still Did Not Stop Selling. The Initial Opening Price of Bullion Was 42 Taels and a Half, Slightly Smaller by 1 Taels and a Half. Because the U.S. Silver Shrank and Was in Short Supply, People's Hearts Were Calm. Next, It Was 50 Taels and 0.05 Mace, Because the Dalian Group and Others Were Competing to Buy. Suddenly, It Was Heard That Someone Named Wu Was Selling, and Various Firms Followed Suit and Disposed of Their Holdings. The Shilling Tended to Be Deficient, Plunging by Around 30 Taels, Counting as 21 Taels. Later, the Buyers Took Advantage of This to Buy, Rising More Than 10 Taels Again. The Afternoon Turned From Firm to Withered, But It Was Confused and Shapeless, Falling From 38 Taels and a Half to 29 Taels. The Closing Price Was 33 Taels and 1 Mace, Falling Back by 1 Taels and 0.09 Mace Compared to the Previous Day. There Was Also a Difference of 29 Taels and a Half in One Day. Various Firms' Supply Exceeded Demand. On Thursday, the Large Bar Slightly Rose by 0.0125, and the U.S. Silver by 0.0375. The Exchange Rate Suddenly Increased by Two and a Half Blocks. Chinese Merchants Still Mainly Sold. As for the Gold Market, It Continued to Show Weakness and Fatigue. The Opening Price Was 29 Taels and a Half. After That, Storms and Tumults Arose, and the Air Was Floating. There Were One or Two Taels of Rebounds From Time to Time, and It Was Sold by Major Players. Suddenly, It Had Broken Through 700 Taels, to 698 Taels. The Noon Closing Rebounded to 07 Taels and a Half. In the Afternoon, There Was News of France's Discussion of War Debts. The Market Knew All About It Again, and Suddenly Increased by 10 Taels, to 14 Taels. It Returned to 04 Taels and a Half Because There Were More Sellers. The Closing Price Was 710 Taels, Still Slightly Lower Than the Previous Day by 23 Taels and 1 Mace. The Total Day Counted 32 Taels Up and Down. The Storm Was Also Very Large. The Next Day, the Large Bar徵Grew, the Shilling Remained Unchanged, the Internal Market Was Slightly Firm, and Fellow Traders Had Some Replenishment. The Initial Opening of Bullion Added 13 Taels, to 723 Taels. After That, There Were Ups and Downs of 10 Taels. Buying and Selling Varied. The Noon Closing Was Flat, Counting as 20 Taels. In the Afternoon, There Was Only a Review of 7 Taels. It Had Been to 17 Taels. The Closing Price Was 20 Taels and 0.06 Mace, Returning 10 Taels and 0.06 Mace More Than the Previous Day. The Fluctuations Were Slightly Calmer. On Saturday, the Large Bar Did Not Change, the Shilling Increased by One Block, the Internal Market Also Loosened, and Chinese Merchants Still Sold Unrelentingly. Suddenly, There Was a Shocking Terrible Drop in the Gold Market. The Opening Price Was 704 Taels. After That, It Fell From 09 Taels Into the 700 Tael Mark. Major Players Sold One After Another. The Exchange Rate Was Especially Weak. Suddenly, It Was 690 Taels and 0.05 Mace. It Was Competed for by Hedging Firms and the Dalian Group, So It Was Pulled Up More Than 10 Taels Again. The Noon Closing Was 702 Taels, Still Falling by 18 Taels and 0.06 Mace Compared to the Previous Day, But the Selling Momentum Did Not Stop. After the Closing, It Was Done Small Again, Four or Five Taels, Only 697 or 698 Taels. In Half a Day, There Were 18 or 19 Taels of Review. The High and Low Prices of the British, American, Indian Silver Markets, as Well as Exchange Rates and Bullion, Are Described Separately Below.

Large Bar and U.S. Silver Soar 161

Yesterday (June 28), a Telegram From London Said That China Was Eager to Buy at High Prices, and the Market Was Very Firm. According to Large Bar Silver, Both Recent and Forward Periods Increased Sharply by 0.0375, Both Were 13 Pence and 8125. Also Received a Telegram From New York, the U.S. Silver Price Increased by 0.0625, Counting Spot Goods as 2 Jiao and 9 Fen and a Half. Private Telegrams Also Increased by Half a Fen, to 2 Jiao and 9 Fen and 75. The Market Was Stagnant. The British Rate to the U.S. Remained Unchanged, 0.0625, Being 4 Yuan 8 Jiao 6 Fen and a Half. The Japanese Rate to the U.S. Was Still 49 Yuan 4 Jiao 1 Fen. The British Rate to Japan Was Still Counted as 2 Shillings 0375. The British Shanghai Shilling Rate Increased by 0.0375, to 1 Shilling 4 Pence and 375. The Bombay Spot Goods Increased Sharply by 17 Anna, Counting as 45 Robies and 9 Anna. The Forward Period Also Increased Greatly by 17 Anna, Being 44 Robies and 05 Anna. The Spot Market Was Firm Because of the Good News From the United States.

Silver Discount Suddenly Rose Sharply Yesterday 162

Related to the Semi-Annual Closing of Accounts at the End of June

Yesterday Was Sunday, and Banks Were Closed as Usual. However, in the Money Market, Because the Banks Were Closed and It Was Approaching the Semi-Annual Closing of Accounts at the End of June, the Demand for Funds Was Inevitably Greater Than the Supply. Therefore, They Competed with Each Other. As a Result, the Silver Discount Increased More Than 1 Qian Compared to the Previous Day, Counting the Early Market as 1 Qian and 8 Fen, and the Noon Market as 1 Qian and 6 Fen, Setting a New Record Unseen in Recent Days. The Market Price of Foreign Cents Mostly Remained Calm as Usual. The Early Market Was Counted as 7 Qian 2 Fen 7 Li, and the Noon Market Was 7 Qian 2 Fen 7 Li 2 Hao and a Half, Making Transactions. The Early Market Transferred 890,000 in Funds, the Noon Market 440,000. Banknotes Only Made Transactions of 50,000 in the Noon Market Outside the Market, and 35,000 in the Noon Market. Bank Transactions and Receipts Were Silent Due to the Closure and Suspension of Business. Money Shops Received and Resolved More Than 7.4 Million in Foreign Public Orders and More Than 43 Million in Silver Public Orders. The Exchange of Funds From Various Routes Was More Than 300,000. Small Money Shops Traded More Than 300,000. In the Auxiliary Currency Market, the Jiangnan Small Foreign Exchange Was 6 Qian 4 Fen 7 Li in the Early Market and 6 Qian 4 Fen 6 Li in the Noon Market, Making Transactions of 3,500 Jiao in the Early Market and 2,500 Jiao in the Noon Market. The Guangdong Small Foreign Exchange Was 90,000 Jiao in the Early Market and 55,000 Jiao in the Noon Market. Copper Coins Increased by 1,000 Wen, to 378,500 Wen.

Last Week's Securities Prices of Bonds Continued to Rise 163

The Prices of Important Bonds Rose Again by Around Two or Three Yuan

The Market Continued to Be Smooth, With Transactions Exceeding 110 Million

Last Week, the Market Conditions of Various Bonds on the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, Although the Futures Market Was Approaching Delivery, Transactions Were Still Extremely Lively. The Market Was Active as Before. Except for One Day on the Weekend, When the Delivery Volume Was Huge, the Market Was Closed Before Settlement to Facilitate Delivery. On Friday, the June Term Was Prepared for Delivery and Bidding Was Suspended, While the August Term Was Not. Only the July Term Had Transactions of 9.4 Million Yuan. The Rest Were Very Prosperous. On Monday and Wednesday, the Two Days Each Reached Approximately 27 Million Yuan. On Tuesday and Also Had 23 or 4 Million Each. It Is Estimated That a Total of 110 Million and 915,000 Yuan Were Opened in May. The Huge Volume of Transactions in the 20-Year Customs Tax Still Far Exceeded That of Local Bonds, Exceeding the Previous Week by More Than 2.6 Million Yuan, Accounting for 39.81 Million Yuan. The Others Were Relatively Flat, and Transactions in the July Term Also Increased. It Is Estimated That 20-Year Cigarette Tax Was 18.705 Million Yuan, 19 Shan Was 12.375 Million Yuan, 19 Customs Was 11.47 Million Yuan, Disarmament Was 11.68 Million Yuan, Compilation and Legacy Was 10.12 Million Yuan, 96 Public Bonds Were 2.735 Million Yuan, Reorganization of 6% Was 2.74 Million Yuan, Customs Tax Was 1.265 Million Yuan, 7-Year Long-Term Was Only 15,000 Yuan. Spot Goods Transactions Were Only 41,000 Yuan, Counting 12,000 Yuan for Disarmament, the Others Were Only a Few Thousand Yuan. Speaking of the Trend of Market Prices of Various Bonds in the Past Week, the Situation Was Good, the Market Was Optimistic, Investment Purchases Were Enthusiastic, and Short Covering Was Still Active. The Buying Momentum Was Strong, and the Rising Trend Did Not Decline. In the First Two Days of the Week, Except for Customs Tax, Compilation and Legacy, 96 and Other Peaceful Ups and Downs, the Rest Rose Sharply. Each Day Jumped High by One Yuan to Two and a Half Yuan. The Rising Trend and the Hot Weather Were Almost Side by Side. Only Wednesday Had a Slight Reaction. Thursday Had Minor Ups and Downs. Friday Also Had No Major Ups and Downs. As a Result, Compared to the Previous Week, Except for Compilation and Legacy, 96 Were Only a Few Horns Better, the Customs Tax Rose by About One Yuan, and the Others Rose by Two or Three Yuan. Also, Last Monday, the Market Was Closed Due to the Handling of the Delivery of June Futures. Bidding for August Futures Only Began on Tuesday. Except That the July Term Had Cancelled the Provision of Actual Products, the Sale of August Futures Was Still Limited to the Provision of Actual Products. Yarn and Cotton Flower Last Week's Bullion Hit Down Six Taels 164

Spot Goods Also Small Three or Four Taels

Three Products Rose Alone More Than Ten Yuan

At the Beginning of Last Week, the Situation of Cotton Yarn Was Firm and the Rising Wind Was Sharp. The Sales of Spot Yarn Were Enthusiastic, and the Intention of Various Groups Was Very Excited. Moreover, 16s and 20s Spot Yarn Had Been Exhausted by Various Groups in the Previous Week. The Bottom Stocks of Various Factories Had Long Been Emptied. The Tianjin Group, in View of the Shortage of Spot Goods, Changed to Purchasing July and August Futures. People's Hearts Were Excited, the Situation Was Tense, and the Atmosphere on the Market Was Especially Strong. Unexpectedly, After the U.S. President Announced the Deferral of War Debt Payments for One Year, the Bullion Plummeted by a Huge 70 Taels in One Day. The Hot Rising Wind of the Yarn Market Suffered a Heavy Blow. At the Same Time, the Selling Momentum Suddenly Became Strong, and Major Short Positions Added More Codes. The Tabletop Suddenly Loosened, and the Situation Changed Suddenly. There Were Rumors in the Market That a Large Long Position Turned to Empty. It Originated From the Fact That the Opening Price of August at the Beginning of the Week Had Seen a Maximum of 169 Taels and 2 Qian. After Suffering Various Blows, the Market Disc Collapsed and Fell for Six Consecutive Days. On Saturday, the Minimum of August Reached 161 Taels, a Difference of Eight Taels and Two Qian. The Speed of the Change Was Shocking. Although the Price of Gold Fell, Overseas Prices Skyrocketed, and the Calculation of the Silver Disc Was Not Cheap. However, the Local Environment Was Poor, and Various Airs Were Conducive to the Short Side. Moreover, Most Tended to Throw Short, How Could the Market Support It. The Spot Yarn Business Was Exceptionally Dull on the Weekend. Although Various Groups Had a Volume of Handling, They Were Hesitant to Move Forward Because the Situation of the Period Yarn Was Unstable. It Was Found That the Statistics of Various Groups Buying Showed 6,630 Packages. The Trading Company Entered 3,850 Packages. Shinren and Zhong Yarn Were Shipped to Japan, One After Another. The Spot Yarn Market Also Fell by Three or Four Taels. Standard Yarn Was Still Firm at the Beginning of the Week. Later, Due to the Increase of Short Positions and the Settlement of Long Positions, the Market Disc Suddenly Turned Downward and the Falling Wind Was Great. The Yarn Market Was Currently Affected by Exchange Rates, and the Gold Market Was Shaky. Although the Future Was Still Solid, the Price of Bullion Was Down by 5.6 Taels Compared to the Previous Week. The Transaction Statistics Were 298,800 Packages. Three Products Yarn Rose by More Than 10 Yuan Compared to the Previous Week. The Package Amount Bought by Various Groups Is Recorded Separately Below.

Last Week's Cotton Market Diverged at Home and Abroad 165

American Cotton Rose 140 Pounds of Sound

Han Standard Actually Fell One Liang and Five or Six Qian

Last Week's Cotton Market, Hit by the Gold Price, Had a Strong Falling Wind. The Yarn Market Also Suddenly Turned Downward, Causing Great Void in People's Hearts, and the Selling Momentum Was Very Strong. Although the Source Was Lacking and the Bottom Stock Was Weak, Hong Exchange Rate Changed, and There Was Hope for the Smooth Entry of Foreign Cotton in the Future. So Speculators Swarmed and the Situation Was Fierce. The Buyer Was Difficult to Support for a While, and the Spot Cotton Needs of Various Factories Were Silent, So the Market Disc Was Tired. Each Month Fell by One Liang and Five or Six Qian Compared to the Previous Week. The Weekend Slightly Rebounded. Although Overseas Silver Prices Rose, Prices Also Rose. The Local People's Hearts Were Poor, and They Unanimously Looked Tired.

Transaction Statistics Were 486,700 Dan. The Source Was Estimated to Be 5,225 Packages of Yao Flower, 500 Packages of Tong Flower. There Were Not Many Transactions of Spot Cotton From Manufacturers. The Food and Rice Market Is Falling Downstream 167

Xinzha Yesterday, About 30 Ships Arrived With Changxi and Clam Subsidies, Etc. The Sales Volume Is Thinner Day by Day Than Before. The Top Goods of Thick Japonica Rice Fell by the Corner, and the Medium-Guan Goods Were All Lower by Two Horns. The Situation Was a Thousand Miles Down. Thin Rice Was the Softest. The Goods Still Poured In. There Were No Sales Routes, and the Market Was Falling Downstream. The Foreign Du Jian Buyer's Sales Site Was Uniquely Prosperous, and the General Trend Was Set. There Were Slightly Fewer High Goods in Bajian, and the Transactions in the Middle Gate Were Scattered. The Price Was Tired, Xu. Rare Goods in the Port Tip Had No Glory or Disgrace. The Source of Guest Tip Gan Wan Was Extremely Rare. The Landlord Had No Intention of Selling Off the Price, So It Was Stable. Glutinous Rice Arrived and Sold Two Enemies, and the Price Did Not Rise or Fall. The River Factory Each Goods Horn Opened About 2,000 Loads.

South Shanghai Yesterday, a Dozen Ships Came and Sales Were Very Dull. Changxi Thick Japonica Softened, Short One or Two Corners. Su Tong Machine Japonica Also Fell Sharply at the Beginning, and High and Subordinate Were Not Prosperous. It Was Slightly Set Until the Noon Closing. The Wind Fell More Violently in the Early and Late Rice of Nangang, Qingpu, Songjiang, Zhangyan, Fenglian, Etc. Each Lowered by a Huge One or Two Corners. The Goods Still Arrived. The Stores and Buyers Here Were Extremely Dull, and the Situation Did Not Return High. The Foreign Du Tip and the Darkened High Fixed Times Were Tired, and the Elephant Downstream. Social News

Legal Person Invents Non-Burning Red Oil 177

Could Prevent Airplane Fires

London News: Mr. Bartel, the technical director of the French Aviation Association, and Mr. Foley, the secretary, have jointly invented a safe gasoline called "Red Oil." When used in airplanes, it can prevent fires. The two first traveled between Bourget, France, and Croydon, England, six times for secret experiments, which lasted two months. Recently, the experiments were supervised separately by the French and British authorities in the two locations, and the results were confirmed to be successful. This non-combustible "Red Oil" is extracted from crude oil to obtain white spirits, which are then subjected to special treatment. It is said that its power is no different from ordinary gasoline. During the experiment, a red-hot iron rod burned in a furnace was immersed in the oil, but the oil did not catch fire, as if it were water, which amazed the observers.

Gospel for All Living Things in the World 178

British and French Parliaments Form Animal Welfare Groups, Anti-Vivisection Sentiment Grows in Austria-Hungary

London News: After the British Parliament organized the Biological Welfare Committee, a similar organization has been established in Paris, with Mr. Herriot as chairman. The British committee recently elected several members to visit Paris to contact the French committee. On the one hand, they persuaded the legislative bodies of all countries in the world to form similar groups, and on the other hand, they sought assistance from the League of Nations.

Also, Vienna News: Opposition to vivisection in the Hungarian medical community is gradually increasing, becoming a powerful public opinion. Vienna established a Doctors Against Vivisection Association two years ago, and now its membership has reached 260, including famous professors such as Professor Lawrence and Professor Zhewosdak.

Discussing Plans to Increase National Poultry Breed Improvement by 280 Million 179

— Wang Zhaotai

The fundamental reason why Chinese society cannot be stable is economic bankruptcy. If we want to build China into a new country in the world, we must transform the rural economy. Recently, Mr. Zhang Ji of the Central Committee proposed that reviving China should prioritize agriculture and treat industry as secondary, which is indeed a wise opinion. However, we who live in cities, although we know that agriculture is important, few of us actually know the real situation in rural areas. Whenever we go to the countryside in any province, we see that nine out of ten households are poor and displaced. Such a tragic image of national demise is truly pitiful to the extreme. However, with such complex and numerous rural issues, it is not easy to know where to start to revive the rural areas so that more than 300 million hardworking, frugal, and innocent farmers can live in a peaceful world. Of course, it is not an easy task. However, we cannot stop our great ambitions because of the difficulties and give up due to minor setbacks. With the spirit of courage and determination, even if the road ahead is full of mountains, rivers, thorns, and brambles, we must do it with the power of our nation. Since Dr. James Yen, the executive director of the Mass Education Movement, advocated that education must be integrated with life, and Dr. Franklin H. Warner used the method of increasing production to organize a new rural Chinese economy as a comprehensive rural improvement plan, conducting experiments in the Dingxian experimental area, there has been considerable progress. For example, the improvement of pig breeds has indeed been trusted by farmers. All other improvements are made using scientific methods to improve agricultural products, which have made a great contribution. We cannot help but admire the far-sighted planning and spirit of sacrifice of Drs. Yen and Warner. Next is the chicken breed improvement that I want to talk about.

Chicken breed improvement is also one of the most important issues in Chinese rural areas. Because raising chickens is so common in China that almost no other country has it. Even the United States, which is called the world's number one chicken-raising country, cannot match the situation in China where every household raises chickens and everyone loves chickens. Of course, there are its special features and benefits, so farmers like to raise them. I will first talk about its importance to the national economy. Chinese people have basically never paid attention to raising chickens, so few people know about it. Every Chinese person knows that Chinese silk and tea are sold to countries all over the world, with huge annual exports, but they do not know that the products of chicken exports are second only to soybeans, silk, and furs. According to the customs report in 1928, egg exports were more than 43 million taels, which is 6 million more than tea exports. The export egg price offset the import of cigarettes, with a surplus of 10 million taels. As the fourth most important product in China, it is ignored by no one. It can be seen that our country does not know how to develop sources of profit, which makes the country poor and weak. It is a pity. This is in terms of international trade. If we talk about national farmhouse production, it will also surprise people as a huge number. According to Dr. Franklin H. Warner's investigation, there are 70,000 farm households in Dingxian. If each household raises an average of ten chickens, there are a total of 700,000 chickens. If each chicken of the improved breed can sell three yuan of eggs, the total annual sales will be 30 yuan. Calculated for the entire county, there is a total of 2.1 million yuan. China has approximately 2,000 counties, and taking the poor and small county of Dingxian as the standard, the national annual egg income is 420 million yuan. Such an alarming number of annual egg values is still sufficient for repaying foreign debt, and even more. Even if this year's Ministry of Finance's 20th annual foreign debt repayment is 70-80 million, the national construction budget is only 6 million, and the education expenditure is 20 million, totaling 100 million, which is only one-fortieth of the production of eggs alone. Therefore, it is said that China's poverty is not impossible to solve. It is because our people are indifferent and do not use scientific methods to improve it. Conversely, has China improved chicken breeds? Dare to say, no. Since it has not been improved, the income is certainly not that much. What is it actually? This research was conducted by Tsinghua University in Beijing, raising Chinese chickens and studying the number of eggs they lay. After three years of experiments, the result was that each chicken laid an average of only 50 eggs per year. If the market price at this time is one yuan per foreign egg, according to this number, each farmhouse is one-third of the above estimate. In other words, the total annual production is reduced by two-thirds. One year is a loss of 280 million yuan in income. If we look at this number, is it not the biggest loss to the country? However, can the production after improving the chicken breeds be sold? We also have to think, is there no way to sell the goods, wouldn't there be a danger of surplus? I will prove with examples that there is no need to worry about selling. The U.S. Department of Agriculture's 1931 forecast of China's cargo requirements published in the Da Gong Bao said, "The demand for eggs will also increase." Although the United States produces more eggs, 400 million dozen more than China annually, it still needs to buy from China. Not to mention other countries. If China produces high-quality products, there will definitely be a shortage of supply. Secondly, the Soviet Union used 1.2 million rubles to purchase 100,000 chicks from China, earning the country 4 million rubles in 1932. This news was published in the Tianjin Da Gong Bao on February 2 of this year. Based on this, China's chicken products will never be unsaleable. Furthermore, as the world's civilization advances, the need for eggs is increasing. The number of eggs consumed by each person each year in each country can be seen:

Canada 313

United States 180

France 133

Germany 117

United Kingdom 110

Denmark 75

Japan 37.5

(Recorded from the Japanese Showa 5th Year Poultry Magazine)

If we refer to this comparison table, we will know that the stronger and more civilized the country, the more it needs. Although we in China do not have this kind of statistics, we think, how much can the average wealthy person use in a year? I think it's very little. Farmers almost don't eat it. This is what I personally investigated. In the past few years, the Japanese Emperor saw that his people consumed too few eggs, and specifically ordered the people to eat eggs every day to nourish their bodies and become healthy people for the country. Therefore, the country promoted chicken raising and the Emperor personally visited various places to show encouragement. This is the forerunner of paying attention to national hygiene. In ancient times, Mencius said that raising chickens and good meat is the foundation of kingship, which is the same reason. If China wants to become a strong country in the world, it must pay attention to national hygiene. I think promoting eating more eggs is a necessary fact. So, why worry about egg surplus?

Based on the above reasons, improving chicken breeds has a great relationship with people's livelihood and the nation. As for the method of improvement, it is to use the world's most productive egg-laying breed, Leghorn. In 1928, only this breed of chicken was distributed to various villages for improvement. The procedure for improvement is to mate one rooster with ten local hens, which is called pure hybrid mating. Secondly, purebred chickens are raised. Now, the advantages of improving chicken breeds are described below:

The improved chicken breeds in the picture above lay an average of 160 eggs per year, while domestic chickens lay only 50 eggs per year, a difference of three times.

Page 20

Two improved Leghorn eggs are heavier than three Chinese eggs, which also increases production.

Improved chicken breeds and domestic chicken breeds are raised at the same time. Improved chicken breeds grow two pounds faster than domestic chickens.

Because of the above practical experimental comparison benefits, I went to various villages to give lectures to make farmers understand, which was very popular among farmers. The picture below shows the farmers listening to the lectures.

Since the lectures, farmers have been asking for improved chicken breeds every day. This is also the application of Dr. Yen's original quality of education, which makes them feel the automatic need, and the future implementation of improvement can be solved easily. Therefore, we first promote women in various villages because women manage household affairs and are the closest.

I have already talked about the facts of improving chicken breeds in Dingxian. Now, I will briefly describe my humble opinions on the national chicken breed improvement plan.

We observe the situation and needs of the countryside and know that chicken breed improvement is a necessary task for Chinese rural villages. However, to improve the national chicken breeds, there must be a corresponding plan and steps to achieve good results. However, in China's current economic situation, the plan must be within a possible range. First, it must require less funding and be successful quickly. Second, it must be in line with China's situation. According to my investigation in Dingxian, each county only needs 1,000 yuan, and after seven years, it can earn millions of yuan in income. I think no other business is as easy as this. However, many people doubt whether this Leghorn breed can live the same life as local chickens. The Leghorn chickens that we have promoted to various villages grow very strong and are even better than those raised in ordinary experimental farms because they are close to nature. Therefore, we have no worries at all. However, China has never had chicken breed improvement since the beginning of history, and no one studies poultry science, in particular. If a business has no scientific research, there is absolutely no hope of success. Therefore, if we want to improve chicken breeds, we must establish a national seed chicken farm, hire Chinese and foreign experts to study poultry science and promotion methods, and raise a large number of seed chickens to be distributed to various provinces. After the national seed chicken farm is established, the agricultural and mining departments of each province will send specialists to learn promotion methods and general poultry science. The specialist will return to his province and distribute a certain number of seed chickens from the seed chicken farm to farmers. At that time, the methods learned from the national seed chicken farm will be used to order the construction bureaus of each county to send personnel to the province to learn, and the seed chickens will be promoted to farmers in each county. In this way, the agricultural and mining departments and the construction bureaus are only responsible for promotion and organizing cooperatives, while academic research still falls under the responsibility of the national seed chicken farm. According to my plan, each county has 100 seed chickens, and after seven years, it can be popularized throughout the county.

Number of Chickens Promoted Annually in Each County

In the first year, 100 seed chickens are distributed to farmers. There is no need to set up a special experimental farm to save costs. In the spring of the following year, farmers are ordered to return 20 purebred chicken eggs per chicken each year for hatching. 20 eggs can get 5 chickens. The chickens obtained are used for promotion in the following year.

In the second year, 500 chickens are promoted (the method is the same as in the first year), calculated by multiplying 5 chickens per chicken in the first year.

In the third year, 2,500 chickens are promoted.

In the fourth year, 12,500 chickens are promoted.

In the fifth year, 62,500 chickens are promoted.

In the sixth year, 312,500 chickens are promoted.

In the seventh year, 1,562,500 chickens are promoted.

Taking Dingxian as the standard, there are only 700,000 chickens in the whole county. According to the above calculation, there are more than 1.5 million chickens in the seventh year. This excess number is reserved for deaths and losses. Therefore, I said that each county only needs 1,000 yuan, which is the cost of purchasing seed chickens. I think no matter how poor China is, it is not impossible for a county to plan 1,000 yuan as a construction project. It is certainly not difficult for the great Chinese government to plan the funding for a chicken farm. Furthermore, there is no cooperative organization for chicken raising in China. If the seed chicken farm stipulates regulations, and each province and county organizes according to the regulations, this can be used as a considerable tax revenue, which will definitely offset the expenses and have a surplus. This kind of business is beneficial to both the government and the people. I hope that the people will not only pay attention to the 100 million U.S. loan but forget the 280 million chicken production. You must know that living by relying on others will not have good results. Although the United States is very friendly to China, we must guard against the deformation of the East India Company. What is said is good, or it may be to sell his silver sales channels. I think it is better to work hard on our own than to borrow money from others.

Written by Wang Zhaotai at the Dingxian Mass Promotion Education Association in 1931.

Youth Forum

To a Friend 180

— Bin

So-and-so,

In the season when the swallows are carrying crimson petals, you are going to leave wearing the solemn mortarboard. I tremble as I write this, and my heart is filled with infinite pain. Moreover, this unspeakable pain cannot be expressed on pure and immaculate paper like a fallen flower bidding farewell to its old branch. You may secretly blame me for these sentimental words. I don't care about these things at all. If someone like me, who is ignorant and unskilled, is gently blamed by you in your wise heart, I will feel infinitely honored. What I fear most is that you ignore me and pay me no attention.

Among the students in our department, you are an outstanding figure. Your elegant demeanor, your brilliant words, and your superior knowledge all fill me with infinite awe. Really, what else can I say to you besides awe? Therefore, although I have exchanged many unimportant letters with you and had some conversations that ordinary people consider extremely ordinary, I have never expressed anything to you. Now that you are leaving this place to take a high-ranking position in the capital, I am certainly even less qualified to express anything to you. I can only show you the same awe as in the past in the depths of my pure and flawless heart with the friendship of a classmate.

The reason why I am writing this open letter to you, presumptuously, is also to write this.

I remember that not long ago, I heard from a teacher that you were going to be the editor of a certain magazine at sea. I was so happy and excited when I heard this. In secret, I just prayed to all things in the universe that this news could be true. I hoped, but stupid me, because my heart of awe for you was too strong, so I disregarded all the trouble and investigated your career prospects, only to find out that the news was about 80% reliable. Because you published a collection of short stories, which was greatly admired by that female editor, so she intended to hire you as an assistant. Really, if this can become a reality, not only would I bless your future, but also the teachers and friends, who would not rejoice for you? As far as I know, you have a strong interest in literature and art, and what has already been expressed is also extraordinarily impressive. For example, in that collection of short stories, the so-called depiction of women has already achieved unparalleled success, and the bold descriptions are enough to captivate young people who love literature and art. When I read it, I can only feel more awe.

Under the Umbrella 181

— Photo by Bing

The day before yesterday, after having some wine, in my tipsy state, I wrote you a letter. The most important thing I wanted to say was that I hoped you could take on the editorship of that magazine. Because that publishing house is the only one of its kind in the country, it's not easy for ordinary people to get into. At the same time, it publishes many magazines, so its future development certainly holds unlimited promise. If you were to work there for a long time, you could also get to know many so-called influential literary friends. If you could achieve the highest literary reputation in the future, it would not only bring glory to our department, but also increase the value of our school many times over. As for me, unlearned and unskilled, perhaps I could receive your kind affection and be granted literary assistance. Therefore, how eagerly I long for you to take on this editorship! Based on your own preferences, there is no reason why this kind of job wouldn't suit you. Someone with your eloquence and ability to handle affairs is truly well-suited to be an official. However, I believe that a university graduate specializing in running in official circles is not very compatible with what we have learned. Although in the current social situation, what we learn is not what we use. If you really become a high-ranking official, someone like me, an unlearned literary beggar, would certainly not be something you would notice. However, in my foolish mind, I will always treat you with respect and awe. Whether I am favored or not, whether I am loved or not, I do not care. In such a complex society, one cannot worry about so many things.

Although our friendship is very ordinary, it often evokes my memories. Most of all, in the past, I was always envying and praising you. Even in front of teachers and friends, I often mentioned you. Indeed, you have many qualities that deserve the admiration of our peers. In class or at meetings, I often secretly admired your demeanor. However, I was afraid that the students would become suspicious of us, which would harm your reputation. Therefore, in the past, I never spoke to you. My deep affection for you was only silently remembered in my heart, and I dared not express it easily. In reality, the respect and love I often feel for you is no more or less important than the friendly affection I have for my classmates. I have no ambition beyond friendship. I can express this to you with a sincere heart. Therefore, I am writing this letter to you openly, hoping that you will not misunderstand me. There is no other purpose.

I remember one day, I was returning from a friend's place, and it was very late. You were wearing a newly made coat and carrying many things you had bought in your hand. Your face, under the lights of the public bus, looked even more beautiful in your youth. The man next to you looked very unfamiliar to me. Because among the students at our school, I had never seen him before. Perhaps this was Mr. X, who wrote the preface for you. At that time, I did not dare to look at you, only nodding slightly. However, my naive heart was filled with unease. Later, I saw the two of you whispering sweet nothings, presumably talking about me. But someone as unlearned and unskilled as I am is not worth your attention at all, is it? When the bus arrived at XX Company, I got off the bus silently and listlessly, wandered to the small red house, sat on the chair, and smoked, feeling that everything was over.

Truly, the heart of a young man is unpredictable.

To tell the truth, it's a long story. On the public bus to our school, especially in the evening, I often met you. I don't know why, but when I saw you, I only nodded slightly, not daring to say a word. It was truly silent and meaningful. You only glanced at me sideways, as if you didn't want to greet me. This not only embarrassed me, but also hurt me. Although our friendship is still very shallow, I am usually not good with words. After meeting you, of course, I could not say a word. Because of this, your intelligent mind and eloquent speech are so worthy of my admiration. Especially your eloquent and unstoppable debate, it truly captivates countless peers.

In the past, although you and I did not have much friendship, I could still often see your demeanor on the tram and in the classroom, which was enough to inspire me a lot. What about the future? It's truly unimaginable. You are leaving our school to take on a high-ranking official position. As for me, I hope to continue on the path of literature and art and take on the editorship of XX magazine. Perhaps we will still have the opportunity to meet in the future, because I am currently continuing this boring life of a literary beggar. If you take on that editorship, I might still be able to get your help. However, I am an "Adou" who cannot be helped. I hope you won't laugh at me.

This time you graduate, I thought over and over and didn't find anything worthy of giving you as a souvenir. If I gave a souvenir, perhaps the students would suspect us. If you don't despise it, then this short letter can be a souvenir of our time as classmates. Whether you are willing to accept it or not, I certainly cannot force it, and I cannot predict it with reason. In the future, although you have left our school and our department, I will always respect you and hope that you can give me some clear spring of friendship to moisten my almost withered heart. That's all. I wish you

A bright future. Your classmate, ○○
